Security Team Captures a Large Gang of Bandits: On the dawn of the 11th, a villager went to the Jinhui Bridge Security Team to report that there were many bandits moving from south to north at Xiangri Bridge east of the town. After learning of this, Team Leader Sun Jiaxiu immediately dispatched more than twenty team members to follow. They encountered the bandits after about three miles. Seeing that they were being pursued, the bandits pulled out their pistols and fired at the team members, who immediately returned fire. After an hour, the bandits were unable to withstand the pressure and retreated. The team pursued them to the vicinity of Zhagang Town in Zhihui County and captured four bandits, Shen Ayou, Chen Shiming, Lu Xiaodi, and Shang Songfengxiang. They brought the four bandits back to the team headquarters and continued to pursue the other bandits. One of the captured bandits, Shen Ayou, is a well-known bandit leader in Nan Yi, and the Nanhui County Government has offered a reward for his capture. He has been brought back to Nanhui County for trial. The team leader interrogated the other bandits one by one. According to Chen Shiming, he confessed to being a bandit and revealed that stolen goods and guns were hidden in the Huanian Temple south of the town and that there were two accomplices. The team leader then personally led ten team members and requested the assistance of Chen Jinfang, the inspector of the County Public Security Bureau, to search and arrest the bandits. They arrested the two bandits hiding in the temple and found eight rifles, two shotguns, two bayonets, one broadsword, and many stolen goods, as well as Qin Zhao, the abbot of the temple. On the morning of the next day (12th), a worker from Qian Guiqiu's house in the 17th district went to the team headquarters and claimed that the two bandits captured this time, Chen and Lu, were related to the kidnapping of the eight-year-old child from his master's house on the 5th of this month and requested an investigation. After repeated questioning by Team Leader Sun, the two bandits confessed that the matter was done by Wang Taosheng from Helan Bridge and had nothing to do with them. The team leader immediately dispatched more than ten team members to arrest Wang Taosheng. Wang Taosheng confessed that the hostage was hidden somewhere in Shanghai and that there were many accomplices. The team leader then dispatched four team members to Shanghai to arrest the bandits. The team leader personally led ten team members and hired a boat to escort the seven bandits and the stolen goods back to the county for trial.

His 64-year-old mother lives with him. He farms seven acres of rented land. At 9:00 PM the other day, he was invited by someone to rob Zou Jikang's home. Eight people went in total. Captain Zhu obtained the confession and prepared a document to send him to the county for trial.

Summary of the County Police Affairs Meeting: The heads of all Public Security branches in Nantong County gathered at the county bureau for a police affairs meeting. The following important matters were resolved: [T13]1[/T] To vigorously advocate for the allocation of public security land tax in the county budget meeting. [T13]2[/T] All branch bureaus must implement financial transparency. [T13]3[/T] The police districts will be reorganized under the overall planning of the headquarters. [T13]4[/T] A request will be submitted to the county government to issue an order to all district offices, stipulating that they shall not overstep the authority of the Public Security Bureau in the future.

Joint Suppression of Bandit Gangs in the Salt and Yancheng Reclamation Area: Bandit gangs occupy the Yancheng, Sheyang, and Henan Reclamation Area. The Provincial Security Department has dispatched troops to join the 133rd Brigade in a joint suppression effort. On the 13th, the military and police forces stationed in the area, along with the Xia Battalion dispatched by the Li Regiment stationed in Tongzhou, are cooperating in the suppression efforts. All areas of Tongzhou are under martial law to prevent bandits from escaping.

Opposition to Releasing a Police Captain Who Violated the Law: The County Rectification Committee opposes the release of Chen Xuzhai, the squad leader of the county police team, because he abused his power and harmed the people while in office, and a large number of weapons and ammunition were stolen by bandits at the Xiyang Dam. The former county magistrate only sentenced him to two months in prison, and he has now been released. The 35th Standing Committee meeting decided to request the county government to severely punish him.

Rugao 82

Bandit Gangs Rampage in Caojiabu: On the evening of the 9th, about 400 to 500 bandits armed with guns came to Caojiabu in the Rugao Matang District, intending to burn and loot. The district office dispatched the security corps to suppress them. The two sides engaged in battle for an hour, killing two bandits and capturing two others. The remaining bandits were defeated and retreated. However, a large number of bandits returned again last night (the 10th), attempting to attack. The district office reported to the county government for help. Upon receiving the report, the county government immediately dispatched troops to suppress them.

Huzhou 83

Zhang Zhengyuan's Family Kidnapped and Two Women Shot: Zhang Zhengyuan, a farmer from Xia Zhuang Village in Guoxi Bay, in the western countryside of Huzhou, had a relatively well-to-do family. At midnight on the 11th, about 50 bandits, each armed with fast-firing guns and wooden-handled pistols, speaking in a Henan accent, suddenly arrived at his house and smashed the door with huge stones. They ransacked the house, taking all the clothes, silk, jewelry, and cash. They also kidnapped Zhang Zhengyuan's young son, Mao Tou. Zhang's aunt, Madam Yu, was shot by the bandits, the bullet entering near her breast and exiting through her back. Zhang's grandmother, Madam Wu, was also injured by the bandits with the butt of a gun. Madam Wu is over 60 years old and her injuries are quite serious, and her life may be in danger. As the bandits left, they left a letter demanding a ransom of 4,500 yuan. Yesterday, Zhang Zhengyuan sent his aunt, Madam Yu, to the Fuyin Hospital in the city for treatment.

Investigation of the Actual Number of House Tax Collection: The Wuxing County Public Security Bureau learned that the house tax has always been collected monthly by the various branches and remitted to the Finance Bureau for collection. The bureau had no way of knowing exactly how much was collected each month. Yesterday, it ordered the heads of all branches to quickly investigate and truthfully report the amount of house tax that should have been collected in June and July, as well as the actual amount collected.

Ningbo 84

Cai Bojun Shot by Bandits: On the evening of the 11th, 13 bandits suddenly arrived at the Caijia area of Shushan, Cixi. Four of them were wearing long white summer cloth gowns, and nine were wearing short clothes, speaking in varying northern Yuyao accents. The four bandits in long gowns went directly to the Longshan School and met with Hong Ajun, a teacher at the school. Ajun seemed to know the four men and entertained them warmly. Soon after, Ajun accompanied the four men to the security team headquarters of Sujia and the Dongcai substation of the team, confiscating all the firearms and distributing them to the men in short clothes. Ajun then led the way to the house of Cai Bojun, a wealthy man in Sujia. Ajun opened the main door, and the bandits rushed in. Cai Bojun happened to be having dinner with four guests, Yang Qi and Mr. Qian. Sensing that something was wrong, he tried to stand up and escape, but a bandit fired a shot at him, the bullet entering his left chest. At that time, Wang, the squad leader of the security team, arrived from Dongcai and patted a bandit on the shoulder, saying, "Who exactly are you?" He then grabbed the bandit. The bandit, in desperation, fired a shot at Wang, the bullet entering his back and exiting his front chest, causing him to collapse in pain. Taking advantage of this opportunity, Bojun escaped into the next room and hid in a pile of wine jars. At this time, the security team members heard gunshots inside the house and began banging on gongs outside the door. The bandits were alarmed and dragged two guests, Qian and Yang, forcing them to lead them to the Jiuli Mountain in Yuyao. The two men had no choice but to comply. After exiting the house, the bandits saw many villagers and fired their pistols several times, causing the villagers to scatter and hide. Along the way, the bandits searched the two men, taking all their silver dollars and steel watches, and beat and kicked them. They escorted them for five miles to the railway tracks before waving their hands and ordering them to return. Squad Leader Wang was seriously injured, and his life may be in danger. The wealthy Cai Bojun hired a boat yesterday morning to come to Ningbo and was taken to the Huamei Hospital for treatment.

Bengbu 85

Fengyang Customs to Solicit Tobacco Bond Sales: The Ministry of Finance has issued the 19th Year Tobacco Tax Bond. Minister Song telegraphed to the Fengyang Customs Commissioner to solicit bond sales, with a quota of 100,000 yuan. Customs Commissioner Lu Bin has received the telegram and is now complying.

Water Police in the Third District Demand Salaries: The Third District Office of the Changhuai Water Public Security Bureau, located in Zhengyangguan, headed by Director Meng Zhaowen, had a small number of police officers who gathered a few days ago to demand the seven-tenths of their salaries that had not been paid. The situation was very tense. The guards in the office raised their guns in a show of force, causing a gun to discharge and injure a local civilian. Shao Qiyong, the director of the Water Public Security Bureau, has reportedly sent people to investigate the matter yesterday after receiving the report.

Hefei 86

Sharp Drop in Rice Prices in the Last Three Days: When rice was expensive this spring and summer, it cost 25 yuan per shi (unit of dry measure). After the early rice harvest was particularly abundant, the price dropped to 14 yuan per shi. However, in the last three days, due to the increasing supply exceeding demand, the price has fallen again to 8 yuan per shi and is still declining. There is hope that it will eventually fall to 5 yuan per shi.

Joint Establishment of a Self-Defense Committee: Various public organizations have noted that the personnel and administration of the local people's self-defense corps have been sometimes controlled by officials and sometimes by the people, without a consistent system, making it difficult to develop. Now, seven organizations, including agriculture, industry, commerce, youth, women, and the five-district security organizations, have jointly established a self-defense corps committee, electing Fang Xingqiao, Wu Qingcheng, Liu Qingkang, and four others as members, forming the highest authority for personnel and administration of the self-defense corps. They have drafted simple regulations and submitted them to the county government for record.

Letter

Letter from the General Hospital of the General Headquarters: 87

Dear Editor, Yesterday (the 11th), your newspaper published a Hangzhou news story about a conflict between wounded soldiers from the Rear General Hospital and the Jianqiao police, stating that the police fired shots to stop the wounded soldiers from seizing firearms, which is not consistent with the facts. The incident began when a wounded soldier paid for goods at the Yushengyong Department Store on Jianqiao Street with a small nine-year coin worth two jiao (unit of currency). The store demanded an exchange. The wounded soldier, having no change, took out a five-yuan banknote from the Central Bank and asked for change. The store refused, claiming they had no silver to give as change. Both parties then took back the goods and banknote. The wounded soldier then went across the street to a grocery store to buy goods, paying the same price with the original coin and taking the goods. He returned to the Yushengyong Department Store to question why they did not accept the copper coin. There was a slight argument. If the policeman on duty at the time had mediated properly, the situation could have been resolved. Unexpectedly, the policeman only knew to protect the store and scolded the soldier for trying to buy by force. Many wounded soldiers watching from the side were dissatisfied and argued with the policeman. The policeman, realizing that he had incited public anger, panicked and rushed back to the police station to report to Chief Yu. Chief Yu immediately dispatched all the police officers with loaded weapons to suppress the crowd. At that time, the deputy director of our hospital, Feng Ziqiang, Wang Richu, Cai Xiangfan, Yang Genyuan, and others had already led a squad of security personnel stationed at our hospital to persuade and dissuade the wounded soldiers from advancing towards the hospital. If the police had withdrawn completely at this time, the conflict would not have occurred. Unexpectedly, the police thought that they could strengthen their position and prepared to shoot. The wounded soldiers, seeing this, became furious. Deputy Director Feng and others were blocking the wounded soldiers from advancing when the police opened fire from behind, making it impossible to stop the incident. Therefore, the police side should bear full responsibility for this unfortunate incident. In short, since the deputy director of our hospital had led a team to the scene to stop the incident, the police should not have opened fire on unarmed wounded soldiers. The facts of their improper handling of the situation are undeniable. Now, in addition to organizing an investigation team with the military and police authorities to clarify the truth and conduct investigations, we have also sent a letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to send personnel to participate in order to ensure fairness. We are sending this letter for correction and hope that it will be disclosed to avoid the spread of misinformation. We hope for your cooperation. [Signed] The General Hospital of the Army, Navy, and Air Force General Headquarters. August 13th.

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Revises Party Principles and Science Credits for Senior and Junior High Schools 88

And Increases the Total Number of Credits for Senior and Junior High Schools

The Ministry of Education yesterday issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to revise the Party principles and science credits for senior and junior high schools, as well as the total number of credits for senior and junior high schools. The original order is as follows: The Ministry's Small and Medium School Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee previously determined that the study time for Party principles courses in senior and junior high schools should be one credit per week, totaling six credits over three years. The total number of credits for junior high school was 180, and the total number of credits for senior high school general science was 150. The Ministry has already issued orders for implementation. Now, according to the committee's decision, the Party principles course in both senior and junior high schools will be revised to twelve credits, with the time remaining the same. The total number of credits for junior high school will be increased to 186, and the total number of credits for senior high school general science will be increased to 156. This should be implemented accordingly. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued to instruct compliance.

Ministry of Education Interpretation

Graduation Qualifications for the Higher Class of Jing Shi University 91

The Ministry of Education replied to the Ministry of Personnel regarding the nature and graduation qualifications of the Higher Class of the former Qing Dynasty Jing Shi University, stating: According to the letter, please clarify whether the graduation qualification of the Higher Class of the former Qing Dynasty Jing Shi University is equivalent to the current system's university preparatory course or comparable to graduation from a specialized school. The university preparatory course and the Higher Class attached to the former Qing Dynasty Jing Shi University were both established as preparations for entering the undergraduate program of the university. Although there were differences in the years of study, the Higher Class had a three-year study period, and the university preparatory course initially had three years, but was later changed to two years. The nature of the two was the same, and the graduation qualifications of the two can be considered equivalent. The graduation qualification of the aforementioned Higher Class (which can be considered equivalent to graduation from a university preparatory course, as mentioned above) cannot be compared to graduation from a specialized school. The former Beijing Government's Ministry of Education has previously replied to the same government's Ministry of Personnel with a record. The original letter stated that the entrance qualifications for university preparatory students and specialized school students were the same, but the curriculum of the university preparatory course was very different from that of the specialized school. It was deemed inappropriate to consider it equivalent to graduation from a specialized school. The Ministry of Education considers this explanation appropriate. The reply is hereby sent for your information. It is also noted that the University Organization Law and University Regulations do not have provisions for a university preparatory course, and it is not part of the current system. Please also note.

Ministry of Education Interpretation of the Departments Included in Senior High School 92

The Ministry of Education, according to Zhejiang University's request for an interpretation of whether the senior high school stipulated in Article 3 of the University Regulations includes both general and vocational departments, has recently designated the school to state: The senior high school mentioned in Article 2 of the University Regulations includes general, normal, and vocational departments such as agriculture, industry, commerce, and home economics. However, the main purpose of the normal and vocational departments is to prepare students for employment, and the curriculum is different from the general department. Graduates who wish to continue their studies should make up for the basic subjects required for further education at the university summer school or in the general department of senior high school in order to connect. The Ministry is currently drafting the curriculum for the normal and vocational departments. Before it is promulgated, the various specialized schools and above will temporarily allow uniform enrollment of these graduates during enrollment, but they must undergo the same examinations as general department graduates. Those whose scores in the basic subjects are failing will not be admitted. It is also temporarily stipulated that normal department graduates must have proof of serving for more than one year before they are allowed to continue their studies. In provinces and cities with service regulations, they must also submit the regulations to the educational administrative organs of the respective provinces and cities for approval according to law.

Jiangsu Province Awards Agricultural Students 93

In order to reward agricultural students, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines has specially formulated twelve articles of the Measures for the Provision of Rewards, which have been submitted to the Provincial Government Meeting for approval and implementation. Article 1: The provision of agricultural student awards in each county of this province shall be handled in accordance with these measures. Article 2: The agricultural student awards in each county are paid from the special expenses under the budget of agricultural and forestry undertakings, but the amount shall not exceed one-fifth of the total special expenses. The aforementioned awards must be approved by the Department of Agriculture and Mines after being submitted by the county government before they can be used. Article 3: Agricultural students in each county of this province who have the following qualifications may be awarded a reward: 1. Those who have studied in secondary or higher agricultural, forestry, sericulture, fisheries, or animal husbandry schools for more than one year and have excellent grades, as certified by the school. 2. Those who are indeed from poor families. 3. Those who are indeed registered in this county. Article 4: The amount of the reward is as follows: 1. Middle school students shall not exceed 100 yuan per person per year. 2. University or specialized school students shall not exceed 200 yuan per person per year. 3. Foreign university and specialized school students shall not exceed 500 yuan per person per year. Article 5: The distribution standard of the reward is as follows: 1. Middle school students should account for 42 percent of the total. 2. University or specialized school students should account for 35 percent of the total. 3. Foreign university and specialized school students should account for 25 percent of the total. If the total amount of the aforementioned rewards is less than 500 yuan per year, all of it should be awarded to middle school students. Article 6: If there is a surplus in the reward for each level of student according to the previous article, it shall be temporarily kept by the county government and shall not be used for other purposes. Article 7: Students in each county who request a reward must carefully prepare a request form and obtain supporting documents, a guarantee letter, and two 4-inch half-length photos, and submit them to the county government of their original residence in September of each year for review and transfer to the Department of Agriculture and Mines for approval. Article 8: Students who receive a reward must submit a certificate of academic performance from the school to the county government of their original residence at the end of each semester for transfer to the Department of Agriculture and Mines for verification. If there is a transfer of study, it should also be reported at any time. Article 9: Students who receive a reward will have their reward suspended if they fail a subject or drop out of school midway. However, if their grades are excellent in the next semester or they continue to enroll, they may still be awarded a reward with certification from the school. (Article 10) If a student who receives a reward withdraws from school or changes majors without reason, in addition to suspending the reward, the reward that has already been received shall be fully compensated by the student's guarantor. (Article 11) After graduation, students who receive a reward should serve in agricultural, forestry, sericulture, fisheries, animal husbandry, and other agencies in their respective counties for one year and be paid half salary. (Article 12) These measures shall be implemented upon approval by the provincial government.

Yu Binqi Warns Swimmers 102

In recent years, the development of sports in our country has been increasing day by day, and people from all walks of life have risen up one after another like bamboo shoots after a rain. At this time of intense heat, swimming is the most suitable sport. Swimming not only can exercise the body and invigorate the spirit, but also is a supreme skill for saving oneself and others in case of an accident. Therefore, the number of learners is increasing, and the number of drownings is also increasing. The people of the country have not yet paid attention to it, so I have never seen any preventive measures published in the newspaper. If this continues, I am afraid that the number of drownings will be even more unbearable. I dare to briefly tell one or two of the weak experiences I have gained over the past ten years, as follows:

[T13]One[/T] It is advisable to practice swimming in a man-made swimming pool. It is even better to have an instructor to teach. Do not swim alone in ponds, rivers, rivers, seas, etc. in the suburbs. Even if you go, the depth of the water should not exceed the upper part of the neck to prevent accidents.

[T13]Two[/T] Although swimming in the suburbs is a wonderful thing to increase skills for those who are good at swimming, when you want to cross the river or sea, you must prepare a small boat on the side to be careful. Because in the water, the entire tibial veins of the human body are extremely easy to bend. Once the tibia is bent, the person cannot move on their own. Even if you have the strength of a thousand pounds, you can only wait to die. Therefore, Europeans and Americans who swim in the suburbs must prepare boats. We should pay attention to this. According to the above experience, I have gained it from those who were rescued from the water, and I have also encountered it once or twice myself. Fortunately, the water was shallow and I did not die.

A Laughing Matter 106

— Hai Ke

Wife: Why are you so cold to me now? I remember that after we got engaged, you often held my hand.

Husband: My dear, I love you no less than before. Now I have to take care of the housework. If I often held your hand, would you still be able to do things?

A: I saw a pig yesterday and suddenly wondered how many hairs it had on its face.

B: That's easy to know. Next time you're shaving in front of the mirror, count them carefully.

A: I'm breaking off relations with Lao Bing from now on. He's really not a good friend. He has a lying tongue in his mouth, and everything he says is a lie.

B: You can't blame him. Not only is his tongue fake, but his teeth are also fake.

American Woman (hearing the sound of a gunshot at the shooting range, falls into the arms of a young man she doesn't know): Oh!

Young Man: What's going on? Are you dizzy?

American Woman: No, it's just that the sound of the gunshot startled me. I'm so sorry.

Young Man: Don't mention it. Please come to the arsenal tomorrow to see the cannon test. I'll be waiting for you there.

Gleanings from War Zone News 107

— Guo Ren

For three months, the Central Army has fought with hundreds of thousands of brave soldiers in the gun forests and rain of bullets on the Jinpu, Longhai, and Pinghan lines. The tragic scene of flesh flying and blood splashing can be imagined. Therefore, there are often gleanings from the war zone. I have collected a few anecdotes to chat about to relieve the summer heat.

Gifts from the Women's慰勞 Society: The Women's慰勞 Society organized by Soong Mei-ling and others purchased a large number of items in Shanghai and transported them to the front lines for distribution. The staff members also received several boxes. In addition to timely medicines and supplies such as "Flying and Living" [應時藥品], there were also biscuits, small cans of sugar, and soft candies worth one copper coin each. The group laughed and said, "We are not children. Why give us these candies and biscuits? In this hot weather, we would really like them to buy some canned fruit to comfort us."

Commander Gu is well: Gu Zhutong is loyal, brave, and good at fighting, and is relied on by Chiang Kai-shek. Previously, various foreign newspapers widely reported that Gu was seriously injured and killed in battle. This was actually a false rumor. Now, Gu is fighting bravely on the Longhai front line. It can be seen that Commander Gu is indeed well.

The Chinese Soldier in the Mouths of Foreigners: A certain division of the Central Army has neat military appearance and complete weapons, which is the crown of all divisions. However, its combat effectiveness is far inferior. Therefore, a certain foreigner jokingly said that this army can only fight foreign soldiers and is not enough to fight Chinese soldiers. The courage of our soldiers to sacrifice and fight and their spirit of enduring hardship are enough to make foreigners admire and be frightened. Foreign soldiers are mostly pampered and rely on the novelty and sophistication of their weapons to use scientific warfare methods. In terms of the strength and solidity of the soldiers' fighting power, they are far inferior to ours. A certain foreigner's words have already revealed their true colors.

Sesame Cakes and Fried Dough Sticks Rolling on the Ground: Once, Feng Yuxiang's plane dropped bombs on Liuhe, which missed Chiang Kai-shek's train and instead bombed nearby vendors, causing several people to be killed or injured. As a result, the sesame cakes and fried dough sticks that these people were waiting to buy with their baskets rolled all over the ground. Also, an old man with a white beard happened to be holding a grandson sitting at the door and was also killed, sitting upright in his chair and dying. The white-haired old man and the yellow-mouthed child died together. The scene was extremely tragic.

The Spectacle of Anti-Aircraft Guns: Anti-aircraft guns are a weapon to defend against aircraft. However, the aircraft soar in the sky and it is difficult to hit them. When the shells are fired into the sky and explode, the black smoke lingers and slowly enters the clouds. It is truly a spectacle.

A Record of Visiting the Empress of Japan 108

— Xin Wei

In recent years, shipping companies from the United Kingdom, Japan, and the United States have been competing for the right to navigate the Pacific Ocean, and the period of general mobilization has become a period of fighting with swords. The Changxing Company spent 2 million pounds, equivalent to 37.8 million yuan in Chinese currency, to build the Empress of Japan, an unprecedented giant ship in the Far East. On its maiden voyage to Zhongkan the other day, it invited people from all walks of life to visit it. There are many interesting things to say about it. Now I will record them as follows:

A Grand View of Female Guests: The Empress of Japan has a displacement of 39,000 tons. Including the cargo hold, it is divided into ten decks. Its height is actually enough to be compared with the Sincere and Wing On buildings. The company issued many invitations, and many Chinese and foreign people from all walks of life who admired its name went to see it. On that afternoon, at 2:00 p.m., they gathered at the Customs Wharf and boarded four small boats, all of which were crowded. There were more than a thousand guests, half of whom were women. Their clothing was all kinds of red, green, flower, and plain, which was a grand and dazzling spectacle. According to Ping Yuanqu's statistics, chiffon qipaos accounted for the most, and the most eye-catching were two aristocratic and fashionable Western women who wore colorful chiffon dance dresses, and their natural bare feet did not wear stockings. It is said that women's dress without stockings is the most fashionable in Western countries. The two women attracted the attention of all Chinese men and women on the ship. It is expected that the women in Shanghai will definitely compete to imitate them.

The Splendor of the Cabins: The splendor of the first-class cabins of the Empress of Japan can be called invincible in the Pacific. The glass garden, grand hall, dining hall, etc. are all built with granite and decorated with colorful paintings, like a royal palace hall. A huge painting hangs on the building, depicting a Chinese story of hundreds of officials paying homage to the emperor, which is ancient and fragrant and can highlight the ancient civilization of the East. The four sides of the hall are large glass cabinets displaying high-end clothing, shimmering with ten colors and five lights, like an exhibition. The most amazing thing is that each room has a fan without blades, which is an automatic hole pipe that uses the natural wind of the sea surface to allow people to be free from heat. The layout of the radio music station is even more dazzling, with a golden ball placed on top and a sound machine below.

Small Boats Racing: The fastest ship from Shanghai to Wusong takes an hour and a half. The small boats sent to pick up the guests that day were all the first-class ships of Jardine Matheson. Because the round trip was limited, they all opened up fast speeds and galloped at full speed. At first, the boats went side by side, not giving way to each other, like dragon boat racing on the river. That day was very hot, and once the boats started, there was a cool breeze. On the way back, the waves splashed many of the fashionable female guests on the outer deck, soaking them like chickens that had fallen into the water. When they returned to Shanghai, the lights of thousands of homes were already lit, and the Customs bell had already chimed eight times.

The Enormity of the Ship: The Empress of Japan is the largest ship in the Far East. The bow of the ship is open and can be used for horse racing. The ship has a total of more than 500 crew members, sailors, and tea boys, and can carry more than 2,000 first, second, third, and steerage passengers. The food used for a round trip to Zhongkan is truly amazing. It requires ten cows, 60,000 eggs, one ton of sugar, tens of thousands of various small birds, and even more milk and flour than can be described.

A Record of Seeking Coolness in Hot Wuhu 109

— Ji Ji, sent from Wuhu

Although the hurricane has passed for many days, the heat has not decreased much. The heat this year does not necessarily start from Wuhu. I am in Wuhu, speaking of Wuhu, but only a part of it.

There are few places in Wuhu that can escape the heat. During the day, the sun god is in power, and it is really impossible to find a place to hide. Fortunately, the government office only handles affairs in the morning, and stops due to the heat in the afternoon. However, they can only sit dry in their residences, reading books and newspapers. After 5:00, when the heat slightly subsides, they often go out to seek coolness. Therefore, tourists gradually gather in places such as the Grand Garden and Little West Lake, and the seats in the cool drink rooms of Mimi Paradise and Henry Jingjing are also full.

The Grand Garden is about ten acres in area, facing Zhongshan Road and backing Taotang Lake (there is a small lake in Wuhu City, with a circumference of only two or three li, some say that it is named Wuhu, but the locals call it Taotang Lake). It is the park of the Wuhu people. It is heard that the Li family of Hefei operates four or five waterside pavilions that also sell Chinese food, but it is very barren, and walking among them makes people feel unhappy. The Municipal Preparatory Office should slightly renovate and stipulate regulations for this only park for the Wuhu people, or sell tickets daily to show restrictions. It is not impossible, otherwise, it would be a pity to sit and watch this great garden become full of scars. It is hoped that the principals will not ignore it and create happiness for the Wuhu people. The expensiveness of the Chinese food in the Grand Garden is shocking. A plate of lotus root is sold for 3.6 cents, and a bowl of diced chicken is as expensive as 9.9 cents. Temporary business is often like this (because it is only in summer and not in winter), which is also a bad habit of the Chinese people.

Little West Lake faces the Grand Garden across the lake, and it also sells tea and wine. The business is not bad, and the price is slightly cheaper. Another room is opened as a Qingyin teahouse. In the evening, from 8:00 p.m., there are more school singers who come from Nanjing. Jin Liangyu, who came from Shanghai, is heard to have sung in the Tianyun Building in Shanghai before. The beard student of the Sun School sings operas such as Xiaoyaojin and Shanchantai. His voice and pronunciation are very pleasant. The Jiang Hongyan and Hongyun sisters often sing together, such as Nantianguan and Wujiapo, which are quite collectible. Ai Xiangnu is a fourteen-year-old girl who can sing new songs such as Drizzling Rain and Grape Fairy, which is like a vegetable and fruit mixed in with a big meal, fresh and lovely. However, her pronunciation of Mandarin is inaccurate, which is her big problem. The songs of Jin Hui are all sung in Mandarin, which is the standard. Although Ming Hui's songs are half in voice, half of them also benefit from the pronunciation of Mandarin. Each guest sells tea for 3.5 cents, and they also order plays. It is heard that each act is a silver cake a day for the singers and the venue owners to share. I once went with Bi Jisen, the brother of the Transportation Bureau, but because I was still suffering from the heat, I did not finish the show. I bought a small boat and swayed in Taotang Lake, and I felt a slight breeze. When I parked near the teahouse, the chirping songs were not different. Soon after, I put myself in the teahouse and heard that there were a total of fourteen small boats in the whole lake. In addition to carrying passengers across the lake (such as from the Grand Garden to Little West Lake, you can take a ferry), the cost per hour is four or five silver tickets (silver corners are not available in other places, and only silver coins from the China Communications Bank are used in addition to copper coins), which can be used to buy a boat, which is also a pleasure in summer.

Others such as First Spring, First-Class Fragrance, and First Happy Spring have waterside pavilions, but they do not entertain those who do not drink and feast among them. The ice drinks of Mimi, Jingjing, and Henry Paradise, Henry is the most high-end.

New Knowledge for the Family 110

— Tian Xu, I Live and Edited

Snowflakes are the most difficult to make. All books on fragrances and cosmetics contain their methods of making them, and they are all different. Trying to make them according to the books is always successful, but it is also always a failure. Because after they are made, they change again, either spitting water and turning yellow, or drying out and hardening. People all think that it is not difficult to adjust the amount of water, but they do not know that the first disease is that the raw materials used are all sodium silicate and alkali. The first step is fundamentally wrong. How can you make the product good? Only by using dry casein raw materials, adding water and boiling, you can succeed. Each pound of dry casein used to sell for one yuan, which can be made into ninety-six taels of snowflakes. This year, foreign exchange has soared, and the price of sodium silicate and alkali has also soared. However, the price of Invincible brand cheese is still one yuan per pound, which is very convenient for small craftsmen. Many remote ports have already sent letters by post to buy and learn the manufacturing method, which is especially simple and appropriate, and can be learned without learning. It is the most convenient for family industry. Between Jiangsu and Zhejiang, in late autumn and early winter, young girls often carry baskets and sell snowflakes stored in glass jars, full of fragrant snow, crystal clear and shining like silver, which can be seen at a glance to be made by Invincible brand casein. It is as soft as Summer's Eve and has good quality and low price, and it will never change. Therefore, it is welcomed by people. Only the longer it is stored after it is made, the more radiant it will be. Therefore, it must be prepared as much as possible after the beginning of autumn to supply the market in a city. (Xu)

White deerskin shoes often need to be wiped with dry powder bags after wearing, but they are always gray and yellow and cannot be as white as when they are new. If you pay the shoe store to wash them, you have to pay half a yuan. Now I have learned a method of washing them myself. Dip a piece of gauze in water and wash them with Invincible brand toothpaste. You must wipe the four weeks of the shoe surface until it is wet. It doesn't hurt to remove the shoelaces first. After it is dry, wipe it with dry powder, and it will be as good as new. You can also use whitening powder to wash white canvas shoes, but it is not as good as toothpaste. This washing will not damage the shoes even if you do it many times, but you must wash the whole body with powder (the soles of the shoes should not be touched by water). If you accidentally dye a stain, you will see water marks instead. (Gu Qingyao)

Tracing the Origins of the London Naval Treaty and Japan's Supreme Command Problem 111

— Ai Ai, sent from Japan

Due to the establishment of the London Naval Treaty, a dispute arose in Japan regarding the government's decision on national defense forces and the military's problem of the Supreme Command, forming a confrontation between the military and the government. Now that Vice Minister of the Military Affairs Ministry, Suematsu, has been replaced and Minister of the Military Affairs Ministry, Kato, has also resigned, it seems that the personnel changes in the navy have come to an end on the surface. In fact, Japan's political turmoil is still brewing. The day of the outbreak is enough to put the Hamaguchi cabinet in a dangerous situation, and it is very important for those who care about the Japanese political situation to pay attention to. Therefore, I will make a more systematic report on the problem of the Supreme Command, which I hope will be welcomed by readers.

The formulation of the Japanese Constitution and the establishment of the cabinet system coincided with the period when Bismarck of Germany was in power and militarism was prevalent. Japan was originally a country that worshipped warlordism. The so-called Japan is the Germany of the East. Not only do countless scholars in the world criticize Japan in this way, but the Japanese people also gladly accept this most glorious and supreme title. Therefore, all Japanese political systems are modeled after Germany. However, military orders and military administration were not detailed and clearly stipulated due to the simplicity of the wording of the Constitution. However, according to past customs, the military has been independent of the cabinet's authority. All matters concerning national defense are the responsibility of the Military Affairs Ministry, and the cabinet has absolutely no right to interfere in this Supreme Command. However, the current cabinet, in order to make up for the failure of the plenipotentiary in the London Conference, actually ignored the opinion of the Military Affairs Ministry and issued a response, which aroused the dissatisfaction of the Military Affairs Ministry, which believed that such behavior was trampling on the Supreme Command and clearly violated the Constitution. According to the view of Minobe Tatsukichi, an authoritative constitutional scholar in Japan, the great power of the organization of the navy and army is clearly different from the great power of the command of the navy and army. The Supreme Command can be separated from general government affairs and placed outside the jurisdiction of the government. However, regarding the right to organize, its nature must be a part of government affairs and must belong to the responsibility of the ministers of state. The organization of the navy and army is related to the facilities of the navy and army's military preparations, and the act of determining how many troops the country needs. As for the government's decrees and the activities of the army, it is appropriate to leave them to the command of the navy and army themselves, without outside interference. The organization of the navy and army involves many aspects of financial and diplomatic relations, so it cannot be entrusted to the activities of the navy and army themselves. The Constitution stipulates individual clauses regarding the command and organization of the army, which is due to this individual nature. Ito Hirobumi's interpretation of the Constitution regarding the command of the army exclusively belongs to the great orders of the military headquarters. On the contrary, regarding the organization of the army, it is said that it originates from the assistance of the responsible ministers. Now, in our country (Japan claims), the so-called independence of the Supreme Command is recognized, which refers to the command and leadership of the navy and army's activities being separated from the government and independent. As for the power of the organization of the navy and army, it does not belong to its scope at all, but is the responsibility of the cabinet, which has the power to assist. According to his words, the Japanese government's recognition of the US-Japan compromise plan at the London Conference was originally a matter of the army's organization and did not need to be approved by the Minister of the Military Affairs Ministry. It cannot be said that the Hamaguchi cabinet infringed on the independence of the Supreme Command. In short, in Japan today, most scholars and public opinion with democratic colors support the Hamaguchi cabinet, while the Privy Council, which represents semi-feudal forces, sympathizes with the military's claims. When the London Treaty takes advisory procedures from the Privy Council, it is still an unpredictable mystery whether the Hamaguchi cabinet can avoid the danger of collapsing.

A Warmth in the Heart (254) 112

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Sows Blessings and Gains a Diamond Ring, and Who Willingly Sings the Golden Thread Ballad Because of This Predestined Relationship

At that time, Zuo Shichen endured his temper and pleaded with the gatekeeper in every possible way to ask the doctor to come out. If he really refused to come out, there was no other way. If he was willing to come out, the consultation fee could be doubled, or any other conditions could be met. He also promised that if the gatekeeper could persuade the doctor to come out, he would give a considerable reward. He talked until his lips were dry and his tongue was parched before the gatekeeper finally agreed to inform the doctor. However, the main gate remained closed, and even the small gate was shut. The gatekeeper said, "Then you stand outside the door for a while, and I'll go ask for you." At that time, it was already late in the eighth month of the lunar calendar, and the cold dew in the middle of the night was gradually becoming chilling. He also remembered his children at home and wondered how they were doing. His wife was helpless, and he didn't know how anxious she was. He stood for more than half an hour before the small door opened again. Zuo Shichen quickly asked him how it was. He said, "I knew it would be useless to run into a wall! I was scolded by the doctor, who said that he had told you long ago that the epidemic is very serious outside now. If it's an emergency, he won't make house calls during the day, and he certainly won't go out at night. Anyone who comes to ask for a doctor should be turned away immediately. What are you asking now?" I said it wasn't an infectious disease epidemic, it was a child's infantile convulsion. He said, "Tell them to bring him over at dawn. Anyway, he gets up very early." At this moment, it was only three or four hours until dawn. As he spoke, he didn't wait for Zuo Shichen to say anything else, closed the small door, and went back to his sweet dreams. Zuo Shichen had no choice but to return dejectedly. He thought about asking a doctor elsewhere, but when he looked at his watch, it was already two o'clock in the morning. Firstly, because he had always been healthy and had no dealings with doctors, he didn't know any doctors well. Secondly, it was already late at night, and there were few families with telephones at that time. By the time he took a carriage to knock on doors and bring a doctor back, it would almost be dawn. However, seeing that the child's condition was getting worse and worse, he had already fallen into a coma. He finally waited for dawn and had to follow the hospital's instructions, taking a carriage to bring the child to the hospital and calling at the hospital gate. At this time, the gatekeeper had nothing to say. Sure enough, the female doctor got up as soon as it was dawn. Because she got up early, the nurses naturally got up too. Appreciating his sincerity, she immediately came to examine the sick child, but after looking at him, she just shook her head and told Zuo Shichen's wife, speaking in a strong Shanghai dialect, "The boy's illness is very serious, very serious." Zuo Shichen's wife said with tears in her eyes, "I only hope that the doctor can save my suffering child." The female doctor said, "It would have been better if you had come earlier, but now it's too late." Zuo Shichen said, "Didn't I come to ask you as soon as he got sick?" The female doctor said, "Yes, but I'm not in good health and don't make house calls at night." At this time, they hurriedly gave the child a lukewarm bath, and he seemed to be a little better.

The Financial and Gold Markets Plunge Viciously 113

Gold Futures Plunge Ten Taels and Five Mace Before Settlement

Selling Frenzy Causes Headwinds for Bull Market Yesterday, the 14th, the spot gold price fell again, and the market suddenly fell into a state of decline. The reason is that the selling pressure suddenly became fierce, and the market sentiment turned from good to bad, which was the opposite of the day before. In the morning, there were more than four taels of ups and downs, and in the afternoon, there were also five or six taels of differences. It was almost time for settlement, but unexpectedly, a drastic change occurred, which was unpredictable. The bulls were greatly hit, and the price suddenly fell by as much as ten taels. The foreign exchange market also seemed to be weak, and brokers such as Hengxing, Senchang, Yongzhi, Fengyong, Yuanyong, and Maoyong sold and bought back, while Fuchangsheng, Dataikang, and Run mainly sold out. Yifeng, Yongshunli, and Hongli all bought in, but the will of each firm was mixed. Although the silver market narrowed in the morning, sellers became brave and immediately moved downstream. After a slight fluctuation, the overall trend was downward. By noon, it had shed more than five taels. In the afternoon, Yifeng, Yuanyong, Xingyong, Taikang, and Run all sold out, while Hengxing, Chengfeng, and Yong bought in, but the market felt even more sluggish and suddenly broke the 70-tael mark, continuing to plummet six taels. The foreign exchange market was quite weak, and the final price was 67 taels and some change. Yesterday, the big contracts all shrank by one-sixteenth, and the silver price decreased by one-fourth.

In the morning, the gold market gradually declined. The gold market for September opened slightly lower by one tael and three mace, with a gross price of 576 taels and eight mace. The gross price fell from 77 taels to 74 taels and seven or eight mace, plus one tael and some change. The exchange rate seemed weak, and banks were doing short-term British gold transactions at six pence one eight seven five. When the shilling was announced, it fell to five taels and one mace, and the posted price did not change. Retail investors also sold. After a while, it increased by one tael. After 11:30, sellers continued to sell, and the market remained weak. At noon, the closing price was 72 taels and five mace, and the announced price was still 625 taels and four mace, with a premium of 62 or 3 taels.

After 2:15, various firms sold out, such as Yuda, Yuanmao, Yong, Xieyu, etc. The exchange market also declined, and the sentiment was particularly weak. Because a certain Chen bought in, it rebounded by two taels at 2:45 to around 72 taels. Later, major players such as Taikang and Run competed to sell, and Sumitomo bought British gold for October at seven pence two fifty and October three one two five, which further weakened the market. As a result, the market was turbulent and unstable, and the waves were overwhelming. It plummeted by five taels and suddenly broke within 70 taels. As it was about to close, it finally fell to 66 taels and eight mace. At the 4:30 closing, it was 67 taels and six mace. Therefore, according to the usual double settlement price, it fell sharply by ten taels and five mace compared to the 13th.

There was a fluctuation of ten taels and two mace. The highest price of the day was 77 taels, and the lowest price was 66 taels and eight mace, with a fluctuation of ten taels and two mace. The posted premium was a little over 67 or 8 taels. The opening price for the morning was 72 or 3 taels, and the afternoon was 67 or 8 taels. A Glimpse of Financial Panic in Jiangxi Province 117

According to news from the financial circles in Jiangxi, some areas in the province have been harassed by bandits, and over a dozen towns have been ravaged. In the worst cases, entire cities have been reduced to ruins. Although other major commercial ports have not suffered disasters, the financial situation is undoubtedly difficult. The funds that have been looted are estimated to be no less than 200,000, and there are still more amounts to be paid within a limited time. The people are impoverished, and finances are exhausted, marking the end of the road for Jiangxi's commercial and financial circles. It is also heard that Shanghai's financial circles have narrowed the scope of business dealings with Jiangxi merchants, collecting outstanding loans and suspending pending loans. All merchants awaiting the transport of goods have sent telegrams to stop transportation, and export goods have also been interrupted, as if invisibly halting imports and exports. As a result, exchange rates cannot be offset by head allocations. Even with the interconnection of Hankou, the potential is limited, as Hankou is now unable to take care of itself. Trading will likely be limited.

Far Month Flour Hit by Foreign Wheat 124

Yesterday, the flour market saw declines in all months, both morning and afternoon. Recovery was difficult because foreign wheat prices dropped by eight or nine dimes, and even a dollar. This led most people to shift their sentiment towards selling. The reason is that those holding on are mostly bulls close to the factories, whose sole purpose is to exploit the scarcity of wheat. However, the northern sales ban on flour prevents smooth sales, so the scarcity of wheat is offset by weak sales. If those with power hadn't been propping up the market, prices could have fallen earlier. Now, with foreign wheat falling for three consecutive days, the near-term market is still being held up due to special connections, while the long-term market is experiencing a significant loss of confidence, and the inverted structure is becoming more pronounced. Looking ahead, if foreign wheat prices continue to fall, further declines are expected. As a result, the current month is down 7.5%, September down 1%, October down 1.75%, November down 1.5%, December down 1.75%, and January down 2%.

Futures Wheat Near Stable, Far Months Down 125

Yesterday, the futures wheat market saw near-term months remain relatively stable, while far-term months declined. The current month initially opened at a high of 5.08 taels, but later retreated slightly as bulls exited. The far-term months saw most people leaning towards selling as foreign wheat prices fell further. If foreign wheat prices drop further and exchange rates align, it seems likely that orders will be placed. Therefore, speculation within and outside the industry suggests that foreign wheat will be the focus going forward. As a result, the current month is down only 1%, September down 3%, October down 4%, November and December down 5%, and January down 3%. The spot market is weak, with factories reportedly halting purchases. Various firms seem to be reducing their positions. Over 4,000 bags of wheat arrived, including wheat from Niuzhuang, Xuzhou, Yaowan, Xinyangzhou, Shaoxing, and Hankou. The 2,000 bags of Niuzhuang wheat were handled by Fuxin, while the rest have not yet been allocated.

Rice Market

South Shanghai

The rice market in South Shanghai for the past two days has seen seven or eight ships arriving from the interior. Market appetite is weak because it's nearing the end of the lunar month. The converted currency goods are scarce, adding more than two jiao to the price. The settled price for regular market top-quality japonica rice is 20.80 to 20.00, green-tip thin rice is 20.90, early rice is 20.40, Tinglin early rice is 20.20, northern converted currency is 18.80 to 18.60, southern port yin currency is 18.00, fresh inside-field rice is 19.50 to 19.30, middle gate goods are 18.20 to 18.00, stale inferior goods are 17.70, Pingwang inferior japonica rice is 17.50, Dacang Mintang rice is 15.25, and white japonica rice is 19.00.

Zhabei 136

Yesterday, five or six boats of fresh white japonica rice arrived from the river, and the price of "Bian Yuan" rice increased, while the rest remained stable. Newly harvested Dongxin rice arrived in small quantities, and rice mills raised prices by one yuan due to the need to fill inventory shortages.

Local News

Zhaoxing Company's Two Steamships Tong'an and Lianxing Collide with Each Other 137

Tong'an Completely Sinks, Losses Exceed 200,000, Four People Missing, Lianxing's Bow Also Damaged

The Zhaoxing Steamship Company's Tong'an steamship was stationed in Chengshan Bay, Haijiao, Shandong when it was sunk by the company's Lianxing steamship, resulting in huge losses. The details of the incident are as follows:

Circumstances of the Collision: The Zhaoxing Company's Tong'an steamship was assigned to sail the Qingdao-Longkou-Niuzhuang route. On the 11th of this month, it departed from Qingdao loaded with passengers and cargo, heading to Longkou. On the morning of the 12th, at 7:00 AM, the ship arrived near Chengshan Cape, Shandong, at 122 degrees 43 minutes east longitude and 37 degrees 22 minutes north latitude. It happened to encounter the company's Yingkou-Shanghai steamship Lianxing, carrying 1,700 tons of coal, sailing southwards head-on. This bay is notoriously difficult to navigate. The last time the China Merchants Bureau's Xinkang steamship sank, it was also at this location. Due to the strong currents and the fog on the sea surface, covered by the morning mist, the Tong'an and Lianxing steamships entered the same lane. When they got close to each other, they realized what was happening. Tong'an tried to retreat, but the bow of Lianxing steamship had already violently crashed into the cabin of Tong'an steamship. After one collision, the two steamships did not immediately stop, resulting in a second collision. As a result, within two minutes, the first two cabins of Tong'an were smashed into two large holes, with the fractures all located below the waterline. After Lianxing reversed, the Tong'an steamship was flooded with seawater and sank, making it impossible to save.

Rescuing Many People Who Fell into the Water: Chengshan Cape is more than one hundred and several tens of feet deep. After the Tong'an steamship was hit, more than 70 passengers and crew members on board fell into the sea due to the violent shock. Fortunately, it was already broad daylight, and the summer heat helped those who fell into the water. Some clung to the steamship body, and others were floating on the sea. The Lianxing steamship quickly released lifeboats and lifebuoys into the sea for rescue, successfully saving more than 60 people on the spot. It is said that four people are missing. It is not yet clear whether the four missing persons are crew members or passengers, as the telegram did not provide detailed information, so it is not known at this time. Whether or not they will be found later has not been reported in subsequent telegrams.

He Xing Rushes to Help: After rescuing the people who fell into the water from the Tong'an steamship, Lianxing immediately sent a wireless message to both the Yingkou and Shanghai companies. The bow of this steamship was also severely damaged due to the two violent collisions. It immediately sailed to Rongcheng Bay and dropped anchor. Later, due to the excessive wind and waves in Rongcheng Bay, the steamship owner feared that danger would arise and urgently changed course to a location 30 nautical miles outside Weihaiwei to anchor for repairs. The Yingkou Zhaoxing General Office received a telegram and urgently ordered the He Xing steamship to rush to Liugong Island to transfer the coal carried by Lianxing and to pick up the stranded passengers and transport them to Yingkou to disembark. Lianxing will be towed to Dalian for major repairs. The losses of the two steamships are roughly as follows: the Tong'an steamship immediately sank after flooding. The crew members and passengers were only able to escape, and all cargo, passenger luggage, and money were completely lost with the steamship. From the time of the accident at 7:00 AM until about 9:00 AM, the Tong'an steamship had completely submerged into the sea, with no trace visible on the surface of the sea. This steamship had a deadweight tonnage of 1,200 tons and was over 30 years old. The steamship hull was insured for 60,000 yuan with Lianbao and Zhaotai in Shanghai. The companies have now been notified. According to Chief Captain Chen Ganqing of the company, the water is deep and the current is strong at Chengshan Cape. It is feared that rescuing the sunken Tong'an will be difficult, and even if it can be salvaged, the cost will exceed the steamship's value, which is not worthwhile. The steamship and cargo losses of the Tong'an steamship are at least 200,000 yuan or more. The repairs to Lianxing will also be quite extensive. The cause of the accident has not yet been reported in detail. It is generally believed that the fog contributed to the accident. In addition, the Lianxing had a cargo capacity of 2,000 tons and was heavily loaded, so the collision caused severe damage to the Tong'an. Both steamship owners are Japanese and have been in their positions for six or seven years. They are quite familiar with the waterways, so the cause of the accident still needs to be investigated.

Overseas Chinese Affairs Advancement Association Urges the Conclusion of a Sino-Siamese Treaty 139

And Requests the Establishment of Consulates to Protect Overseas Chinese

Overseas Chinese in Siam have a long history and a large population. Considering only the relatively high-ranking officials in Siam, whether they are still in office or have retired from war, almost eight or nine out of ten have Chinese ancestry. Even the current King of Siam, Rama VII, himself admits that he has Chinese ancestry, which is generally visible. According to a recent survey by the Siamese government, the number of overseas Chinese in Siam now exceeds 440,000, yet there is not a single Chinese consul stationed in Siam to protect them. As recent news from diplomatic circles reported in various newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai stated, due to the fact that our country has not yet established a consulate in Siam, overseas Chinese who do business or work in that area are often subjected to various abuses and cannot appeal for help. Recently, the Siamese government added a Bureau of Overseas Chinese Affairs, which imposes stricter inspections on Chinese immigrants entering the country. It has rejected the entry of more than 80 people on the pretext that overseas Chinese have contracted diseases. In addition, the education of overseas Chinese in Siam has repeatedly been restricted. They cannot freely develop according to the regulations set by the domestic Ministry of Education, but must be forced to learn Siamese and believe in Buddhism. If the school authorities slightly disobey, they are ordered to leave the country. It is also rumored that the rice business operated by overseas Chinese in that area will be taken over by the Siamese government. If this is truly implemented, the hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese who work in the rice industry will inevitably face unemployment and bankruptcy. Thinking of this is truly frightening. The only way to solve the various crises faced by overseas Chinese in Siam is to quickly conclude a Sino-Siamese treaty and send consuls to protect them. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, the Chinese government ordered Hu Weide, the envoy to Japan, to discuss the conclusion of a treaty between the two countries with Piya Chamlong Ratchakit, the Siamese envoy to Japan. A draft Sino-Siamese treaty was drawn up, but the Siamese government believed that the time was not right, and it was shelved. Compared to January of last year, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Cheng Yansheng to Siam to investigate the national conditions of Siam and the situation of overseas Chinese in Siam. He also made an informal request to the Siamese foreign authorities for opinions on the conclusion of a Sino-Siamese treaty, but there was no clear answer or refusal. The Shanghai Chinese Overseas Affairs Advancement Association has made a special presentation to the Nanjing Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission urging the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to implement the requirements for the conclusion of a Sino-Siamese treaty and to select capable consuls to be stationed in Siam to protect overseas Chinese.

Minhang Seven Public Organizations Request Postponement of House Tax Increase 144

The Minhang District Party Headquarters, Minhang Chamber of Commerce, District Federation of Trade Unions, Agricultural Association, Education Association, Sports Association, and Medical Association, seven organizations in the Minhang District, jointly sent a letter to the Shanghai County Government yesterday regarding the increase in house tax to compensate for public security expenses, requesting a postponement and proposing alternative ways to raise funds for public security. The original letter is excerpted as follows: We are submitting this letter requesting a temporary postponement of the house tax increase and proposing an alternative method for raising funds for public security, hoping for your review and implementation. Our associations recently received Cai, the section chief specially dispatched by the County Public Security Bureau to Minhang, to discuss the matter of increasing the house tax. He briefly stated that although the county's public security expenses had been subsidized by the Municipal Government by half and the number of police officers had been greatly reduced, there was still a shortfall of more than 300 yuan. It was proposed to rectify the house tax to make up for this. At the time, we considered the matter to be of great importance and stated that we would wait for a meeting to gather public opinion and consult with the district office to discuss the matter at length. We have now seen in the newspaper that your government is rectifying the house tax, stating that because the county's public security expenses are insufficient, the house tax in each district should be investigated because the current market price of rent is different from the past. Therefore, it was proposed at the county administrative meeting to investigate the house tax to make up for the deficit. Although the public security expenses have a subsidy from the Municipal Government of 1,800 yuan per month, and the number of police officers has been greatly reduced, there is still a large shortfall, so the proposal was adopted and all districts were ordered yesterday to work with their respective sub-bureaus to quickly investigate the house tax of each household and increase it uniformly this month to compensate for the public security expenses. Although we know that this increase in house tax is actually to compensate for the lack of public security expenses, we find that the county's public security expenses already have a monthly subsidy of 1,800 yuan from the Municipal Government and have been included in the budget for the 19th year. Therefore, these expenses have been secured and there is no need to raise additional funds. Moreover, the situation in each district is different regarding the house tax. Even within the district, the income from the house tax accounts for 80% of the county's total. The district is not the location of the county seat, so the burden cannot be said to be light. Now, using the house tax of the townships and districts to supply the public security expenses of the entire county is probably not fair. Our association believes that public security is indeed very important to local security, and should be prepared by the local area. Our association's idea is that since the Municipal Government already has a monthly subsidy of 1,800 yuan, this subsidy should be allocated equally to each bureau according to the original amount of public security expenses. The shortfall should be raised by each district itself. This method is fairer and easier to implement. If this is appropriate, we have prepared this document to be presented to the County Magistrate for review. We hope that it will be adopted and implemented for the public good.

Correcting the Term "Liquidation" in Store Closures 147

The Accountants Association Issues a Notice to Prevent Social Impact

Recently, the number of stores and companies that have declared automatic liquidation due to losses and entrusted lawyers and accountants to publish announcements has been increasing daily. Among them, some disregard the law and arbitrarily dispose of assets, which often harms the industrial and commercial sectors. The Shanghai Accountants Association has conducted a serious study of this matter many times. In addition to submitting separate requests to the authorities for interpretation and correction of the legal procedures for liquidation and bankruptcy, it issued a special notice to all members yesterday to pay attention to legal procedures. This matter is of great importance to the interests of the industrial and commercial sectors. The notice is recorded below for reference by the industrial and commercial sectors. The notice reads: In recent years, liquidation cases at sea have been accustomed to customs and have not been fully legal. Our members have made corrections and suggestions from time to time. Yesterday, it was submitted to the third executive committee meeting, which resolved that the term "liquidation" commonly used in liquidation cases has no legal basis. It is a simplification of the term "liquidation of accounts," which is commonly used in the business community, and its literal meaning is actually processing due to liquidation. However, its processing method often has the meaning of being similar to bankruptcy but not bankruptcy. It is not possible to distinguish whether the parties concerned should declare bankruptcy according to law, nor is it possible to distinguish whether its bankruptcy has legal procedures. As for its most important part, the liquidation of accounts, it is often ignored. Assets and liabilities often lack accurate proof, and its impact on society is not insignificant. The Company Law only has provisions for liquidators, and the draft Bankruptcy Law only has the name of bankruptcy trustee. There is no name of "liquidation" or "liquidator." According to the regulations on the duties of accountants, liquidators and bankruptcy trustees are all accountants and should be responsible. Our association should actively correct this according to the following methods: (A) Notify all members: [T13]1[/T] When accepting this type of commission in the future, do not follow the custom of using the term "liquidation." Instead, use the terms "liquidation," "liquidator," or "bankruptcy trustee" according to law. [T13]2[/T] All liquidation cases or those whose assets are insufficient to pay off debts and can be declared bankrupt according to law should be carried out separately according to law. [T13]3[/T] A balance sheet of assets and liabilities should be prepared according to law and the responsibility of proof should be borne. (B) Request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the industrial and commercial administrative authorities to issue a notice to merchants not to follow the custom of adopting incomplete legal liquidation procedures in order to correct customs and rectify order. In addition to submitting separate requests to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the industrial and commercial administrative authorities for review and implementation in accordance with the resolution, the corresponding record is sent to you. We hope that your members will follow the above three paragraphs of the resolution in handling this type of commissioned case in the future, so that we can rectify names and manage affairs, and show society the accurate status of our accountants, so that society can firmly examine the careful and legal handling of cases by our accountants, and maintain the appropriate rights of the parties concerned and all related parties, so that we can show great faith and rectify order. I hope you will check and comply with this.

Shanghai County Assists Child Welfare 156

The Chinese Child Welfare Association is now planning to gradually expand its child welfare work to the countryside to broaden its benefits. However, the method of starting must be assisted by Shanghai County, because the administrative scope of Shanghai County is entirely in the countryside, and there are many places where assistance can be provided. The association analyzes that the needs of children in the countryside are slightly different from those of children in the city. Children in the city are more likely to be abused or abducted, and the focus is on protection. Children in the countryside are more likely to be hungry, cold, stupid, and ignorant, and the focus is on education. Therefore, the association asks Shanghai County to assist in carrying out child welfare work in the countryside, with a focus on education. The letter from Shanghai County agreeing to cooperate is excerpted below: We have received your letter and read it carefully. In order to develop international work, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association has always paid attention to the contact with anti-drug organizations in various countries, and has especially worked hard for cooperation with the United States, because the United States' position on limiting the world's drug production is the same as that of our country. In recent years, the United States has also suffered the same harm from the smuggling of European and Japanese drugs as our country. The anti-drug organizations of the two countries have a united necessity for the preparation of the next International Anti-Narcotics Conference to promote the purpose of eliminating drug production. The Pioneer of Buddhist Travelers to the South Seas 161

Recently, three monks of the new Buddhist school, Shi Beiguan, Shi Tican, and Shi Cansan (who had studied at the Wuchang Buddhist Academy, the Zhina Inner Academy, and the Osaka Mikkyo Buddhist Academy in Japan), realized that the life of modern monks does not conform to cultural trends. They specially initiated a traveling group to tour the southern countries, learn from their strengths and make up for their shortcomings, in order to find a new way out for monks. They have now arrived in Shanghai (residing at the Lingshan Temple outside the South Gate) to prepare everything and will depart soon. Here is their declaration: Today's Chinese Buddhism is presenting a scene of decay and death everywhere, a heartbreakingly dark scene. The so-called monks with "worms in the lion's body, turning their heads and flapping their sleeves" are all indulging in sweet dreams, drowsy and confused. Their inherent conscience and heroism have been completely sacrificed in the self-destructive traditional habits of accumulating wealth, indulging in sensual pleasures, and quietly meditating while chanting Buddhist scriptures. Alas, how can this not make people hate the selfless and equal Buddha-dharma, which has become a business for monks to selfishly seek personal gain, a guise to fool devout men and women, and a golden signboard? The so-called sutra-reciting masters who are responsible for the Buddha's life, the sutra-reciting masters who are teachers of gods and humans, it is especially heartbreaking to talk about them. How many people truly possess these qualifications? How many can speak the true dharma? Taking the average sutra-reciting figures as an example, who is not a peddler of Buddhist teachings? Who is not a cheat who deceives the world and steals fame? Who does not have the face of a Bodhisattva but the heart of a Yaksha? Who is not hanging the signboard of a master while engaging in the business of seeking a happy life? Because they are clever and good at seizing opportunities, they constantly update their tricks to confuse you, making them no different from swindlers and traitors to the Buddha. Alas, the inheritors of the Buddha's legacy, the teachers of gods and humans, are like that, what more can be said? Alas, today's Buddhism! Alas, today's monks! However, we are in this situation, with internal poisoning and external oppression, even to the point of death. If we do not quickly seek a way out, we will inevitably perish together. Therefore, we, along with young, energetic, brave, and spirited Buddhist monks in Beiping, organized this traveling group. Traveling is a common practice for Buddhist monks, but our travel has profound meaning, is organized, has missions, and has work (see the organizational outline), which is absolutely different from ordinary activities such as pilgrimages to mountains, worshipping the sea, and wandering around. Now that we are traveling to the Buddhist lands of East Asia, we are not going to travel and enjoy the scenery, nor are we going to see the yellow-robed monks begging for alms. We are seeking the culture we need, the most beautiful thoughts and spirit of East Asia, and the answers to questions that are generally doubted by people in the country today. This is the meaning of our travel. We are extremely grateful for the enthusiasm of the press circles in Shanghai in sympathizing with and guiding us. We will bravely and diligently follow our path and strive to move forward in a down-to-earth manner. This is our declaration. Made by the China Buddhist Traveling Group, August 14, 1930.
