News from Various Trade Associations 167

Chinese Medicine Industry: The Shanghai Chinese Medicine Trade Association was instructed by the Municipal Health Bureau, based on the regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants promulgated by the Ministry, to order the association to instruct all pharmaceutical merchants in the city to apply for registration with the bureau. The association believed that the regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants promulgated by the Ministry were mostly obstructive and difficult to implement. The National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association had urged the Legislative Yuan to promptly revise the new regulations based on the results of the previous petition. All old management regulations were difficult to comply with for the time being, so registration should also be postponed. In addition to submitting a reply to the Municipal Health Bureau, the association also notified the industry as follows: Notification Regarding the matter of pharmaceutical merchants applying for registration, this association previously received a letter from the Municipal Health Bureau ordering all pharmaceutical merchants in the city to comply. After that, it was submitted to the third executive committee for review. All members believed that the order from the Municipal Health Bureau for pharmaceutical merchants to register this time was based on the Ministry of Health's regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants. It was found that the National Pharmaceutical Merchants Association believed that the regulations were obstructive and difficult to implement, so it held a temporary representative meeting of national medical and pharmaceutical organizations in Shanghai last winter and publicly elected representatives Zhang Meian, etc., to go to Nanjing to petition the National Government to request the cancellation of this regulation for the management of pharmaceutical merchants. Chairman Chiang approved the petition and handed it over to the Legislative Yuan for reference. Since the petition, more than a year has passed, and the Legislative Yuan has not yet referenced this regulation. The Health Bureau did not wait for the Legislative Yuan to reference it and implemented it. The pharmaceutical merchants in this city are really suffering from difficulty in complying. Moreover, pharmaceutical merchants across the country have expressed that they cannot accept this regulation. Therefore, the National Medical and Pharmaceutical Association recently convened major pharmaceutical groups to Shanghai to hold a special representative meeting to resolve that, in addition to urging the Legislative Yuan to promptly formulate a unified and perfect management law for Chinese medicine merchants, the current regulations for the management of pharmaceutical merchants are difficult to comply with for the time being. Pharmaceutical merchants in this city should take consistent action with pharmaceutical merchants across the country and postpone applying to the Municipal Health Bureau for registration. In addition to submitting the above reasons to the Municipal Health Bureau to request a temporary postponement of implementation, it is necessary to record the case and notify all my members and colleagues in the city to investigate and comply. This is a special notice. August 14, 1930, Republic of China.

Local News

Roque Formally Apologizes for "Fearless" Case 168

And Declares That the Film Will Be Fully Withdrawn

The "Fearless" film produced by Roque, which has attracted the attention of Chinese people for its insult to Chinese people, was banned from screening by the Shanghai Executive Committee when it was shown at the Grand Theater. The committee also resolved to ban the screening of various films produced by Roque until Roque formally apologized to China. Since the Executive Committee submitted a request to the central government to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to make a stern protest, half a year has passed. As a result of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' protest, Roque has sent a letter to Zhang, the Consul General stationed in San Francisco, formally apologizing and expressing his sincerity in admiring our country. The original letter of formal apology has been approved by the Central Propaganda Department and sent by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Municipal Propaganda Department for notification. It is heard that the Municipal Executive Committee considered Roque to have fulfilled the resolution after receiving the instructions and ordered that all films produced by Roque should be approved for screening after review by the Film Censorship Committee. The Municipal Executive Committee has notified all theaters. However, this matter is unrelated to the Grand Theater case and must be handled separately. The translated version of Roque's letter of apology to Zhang, the Consul General stationed in San Francisco, is as follows:

Roque's Letter of Apology: To Whom It May Concern, I am deeply concerned about the offense caused by the "Fearless" film in your country, Shanghai, which is well known to you. Before meeting with you and Mr. Houston, the Consul stationed in Shanghai, I did not fully understand the reasons for the opposition to this film from the people of your country and how it happened. Thinking about it now, I am extremely disappointed. I dare to sincerely explain the process of filming this film to you. There is only one word that I would like to put forward for careful clarification, that is, the film seen by the people of your country seems to be different from what I saw, which caused misunderstanding. However, I have never dared to harbor the slightest intention to insult the national honor of your country and cause offense to the people of your country. This should be understood first. When the filming of this film began, my manager, Mr. Reddy, hired many experts from your country to provide guidance in order to avoid any damage to your country's groups and people. Even the actors in the film who are from your country were carefully discussed and researched by the aforementioned experts before filming. We have tried our best to be cautious in filming this film. After this film was made, it was shown everywhere here and did not cause any opposition from the people of your country. Even your consulate has never made any criticism. Otherwise, I would have asked you for advice. Therefore, we believe that this film has been recognized as a humorous work. As for whether this film has any intention of being close to insult, I have never thought about it in my heart. However, this film, which has been approved by the official department, suddenly encountered opposition in Shanghai, which is really surprising. The past is gone and there is no need to repeat it. At this time, I only hope that you will convey my sincere apology to the people of your country and ask you to declare that this film has been returned in full because of harmless jokes that have been opposed by the people of your country and will not be shown in China. Finally, I cannot help but say that I am truly an admirer of the culture and art of the people of your country. This time, the stimulation suffered by this film is very significant. Please express my humble sincerity so that I can maintain my friendship with the people of your country. This is my sincere hope. Respectfully, Zhang, Consul General, Roque, September 25, 1930.

Communist Bandits Who Raided Qidong Prison Came to Shanghai for Medical Treatment and Were Arrested 169

He Once Served as a Platoon Leader in the Red Army, and His Gunshot Wound Was Discovered by Detectives. He Was Escorted to the Headquarters for Punishment

The Qidong County Government recently arrested more than 20 communists who had sneaked into the county to plot a riot. After interrogation, three important communists were sentenced to death, and the remaining criminals were also imprisoned according to the circumstances of their cases, awaiting confirmation and execution. The Qidong County Chief also ordered the military police under his jurisdiction to strengthen their vigilance to prevent accidents due to the sudden increase in the number of communists in the prison. Unexpectedly, at 4:00 AM on the 8th of this month, a large group of armed communists came from an unknown source, first firing guns to demonstrate, and then began to rob. The military police were caught off guard and unable to cope, causing the bandits to become more powerful. They forced the police officers of the Public Security Bureau to surrender their firearms and then rushed into the county prison, releasing all 60 prisoners. After the security team encircled and suppressed them, they engaged the bandits in battle and repelled them. It happened that a young man with a gunshot wound to his ankle came to the Nanyang Hospital in the 16th Concession of this city for treatment. However, the young man learned that the director of the hospital was the head of the Qidong Security Corps, so he left without saying goodbye and went to Renji Hospital. The hospital suspected that he had a gunshot wound and did not treat him. Then, he went to the Hui Lü Hospital on Avenue Edward VII. At this time, detectives from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters had learned that this young man was actually a communist from Haimen named Lu Fengyan (also known as Yao Yongdao Yao Binglang). Lu was the commander of a Red Army platoon in the Qidong Communist prison raid and resisted the government soldiers on the spot. His ankle injury was caused by a stray bullet. The next day, he rushed to the Hui Lü Hospital for investigation. It was learned that Lu had stayed overnight and hired a car from the Edward VII Avenue Car Company to go elsewhere. The car company was investigated and it was said that he was now at the Bixin Hospital on Ningguo Road. The detectives, along with Jin Yangwu, a detective from the Pudong Police Station, secretly went to Bixin to arrest Lu and sent him to the Ministry of Works Hospital on Haineng Road for medical treatment. Yesterday morning, the investigating detectives reported the incident to the Jiangsu Higher Branch Court. The police station lawyer, Ru Baoyi, asked Judge Gao to go to the Ministry of Works Hospital to interrogate him. Judge Gao drove to the hospital with the clerks. According to Lu's confession, he had studied for one or two years and his family had 5,000 mu of fertile land (it is said that Lu's confession was purely fabricated). After Judge Gao finished the interrogation, he approved the transfer of the bandit to the headquarters for punishment.

The Bandit Who Kidnapped Liu Nianchun Was Arrested in Suzhou 170

He Was Once a Chauffeur and Fled to Suzhou After Kidnapping Liu

Liu Nianchun, a broker at the Gold Exchange, was kidnapped by bandits at dusk on the 5th of last month at his residence at 921 North Chengdu Road while getting into his car. The bandits demanded 40,000 yuan for ransom. Liu's family prepared 20,000 yuan to redeem Liu, and the kidnapper, Yu Baoren, from Wuxi, fled to Suzhou. He has been arrested and transferred to Shanghai. Yesterday morning, the judge of the Special Zone Local Court interrogated him. According to the police station lawyer, Liu and his wife, Mrs. Ma, took a car out for a cool evening and were getting into the car when they were kidnapped by four bandits with weapons, along with the car. The defendant driver drove to Gongping Road. The bandits drove Mrs. Ma and the chauffeur, Lu Xiangyu, out of the car and kidnapped Liu alone. After the police station received the report, it was learned that Yu Renbao was originally a chauffeur at the Xingxiang Car Company on Disui Road. Two days before the incident, he went to Liu's house to scout. The police station immediately sent detectives to Xinglong for investigation. It was learned that Yu had resigned and moved his family to Suzhou, so detectives were sent to Suzhou to arrest him. The defendant confessed that he was dismissed by Xinglong in May. At the end of June, a friend, Chen Furen, recommended him to go into business and took him to a cigarette den in the French Concession to meet the car owner, but he did not meet him. The next day, Chen asked him to go and drive, saying that it was to transport opium. He did not agree at first. On July 5th, Chen came again and insisted on inviting him. When he went to a cigarette den in the French Concession, he met A Gen and went to a room in a hotel on Sixth Avenue, where there were already five people. They went downstairs together to Xinzha Road. At this time, Chen had already gone elsewhere. The others took out guns and threatened him. He had to agree to help. Therefore, when Liu came out and got into the car, he and others kidnapped him. He drove the car until Huade Road, when they drove him out of the car. He did not know what happened afterwards. Chen had given him 300 yuan and told him not to make a sound. Judge Sun ordered the defendant to be detained for another hearing.

Debate Concluded in the Ge Wei Adultery Case 171

Maid Narrated the Adultery, the Court Ordered a Verdict to be Awaited

Ge Yuming, who previously lived on Hartung Road, had an affair with Wei Suqin, the wife of Cheng Youren, an employee of the China Bookstore. Cheng filed a lawsuit with the former Provisional Court and the verdict was that Ge and Wei were not guilty. Cheng was not satisfied and filed an appeal, and the former maid, Zhou A巧, could testify. However, Zhou was dismissed by Wei and returned to her hometown. Cheng specially summoned her to Shanghai. Judge Feng summoned the maid and questioned her once. Yesterday afternoon, the collegial panel was held at the Special Zone Local Court. Court President Zhou Han was on leave, so Judge Sun Yuan temporarily replaced him as the presiding judge. The appellant, Wei Suqin, was not present. Her lawyer, E Sen, said that Wei could not live in Shanghai after the case occurred and had gone to Nanjing, Songjiang, and other places to seek employment. The appellant, Cheng Youren's lawyer, Xue Jiaqi Wu Chengyu, asked to proceed with Ge's part first because Ge Yuming had arrived in court. The court approved it and summoned the witness, Zhou A巧, for questioning. Zhou, only 16 years old and still a village girl, narrated the adultery between Ge and Wei, which she had seen from a hole in the floorboards above the attic. She also said that Ge would send his servants to inquire whether Cheng was at home before going to Cheng's house each time. If Cheng was not at home, he would come and meet Wei about a dozen times. However, Ge still denied the matter. The lawyers of the two sides then debated each other. Lawyer Xue requested that the first instance judgment be revoked and Ge be punished for adultery because the adultery between Ge and Wei had been proven. The court ordered the debate to be concluded and Ge Yuming was released on bail to await the verdict.

Salt Boat Collided and Sank 173

Loss of More Than 4,000 Gold

Boat owner Pan Youshan transported 550 bags of salt from Songjiang the day before yesterday and sailed to Shanghai. He planned to sail into the sand boat barrier at Dongjiadu in Nanshi to unload the salt at the Gongyonghe Salt Shop, the owner of the goods. At that time, the tide was very high and the boat had not yet entered the barrier when a Nanfang small steamer sped from the north. It was too late to avoid it and it collided violently with the right stern of the salt boat. Immediately, the hull was damaged and water poured in through the cracks. Because the cargo was too heavy to support, the entire boat and cargo sank to the bottom of the Huangpu River. Five men and two women on the boat fell into the water at the same time. Fortunately, they were rescued from the water by the small steamer and nearby boat owners, avoiding drowning. It is reported that the loss of the boat was about 1,500 yuan and the loss of the goods was 3,000 yuan, totaling more than 4,000 yuan. Afterwards, the boss of the small steamer, Zhang Yuansheng, borrowed the salt boat owner, Pan Youshan, to go to the Water Police Station to report the matter. The police chief advised them to go to the salt shop of the cargo owner to negotiate a settlement since both parties were willing to reconcile.

Lightning Struck the Baoshan Electric Pole Yesterday Morning 175

Repaired and Reconnected for Conversation in the Afternoon

Yesterday morning at dawn, the Wusong Fort Taiwan area was full of haze. In an instant, there was lightning and thunder, and the sound of thunder shook the tiles. The rain stopped and the sky cleared. It was learned that three electric poles near the Baoshan Sanguantang were struck down by lightning, charred like charcoal, and the wires were broken, causing the long-distance telephone between Baoshan and Guangfu to be blocked. After the accident, the Baoshan County Construction Bureau immediately sent workers to repair the damaged poles and replace them. In the afternoon, the telephone was back to normal. When the ignorant villagers heard about it, they went to pick up the lightning-struck poles, saying that they could avoid evil spirits. This is not worth laughing at.

Bidding for Ferry Construction Across the River 176

He Xing Machine Manufacturing Plant Wins the Bid

The Municipal Public Utility Bureau is sparing no effort to promote two ferries across the river between the 16th Concession and Lanni Du and between Dinghai Bridge and Qingning Temple in order to facilitate water traffic on the Huangpu River. The three ferries needed were approved by the Municipal Government to be tendered for construction. The bureau immediately issued bidding regulations and publicly invited bids. It was learned that six companies responded, three of which abandoned their bidding rights because they felt they could not handle the job. One company was rejected by the bureau after review. Therefore, only Jiangnan and Hexing submitted bids. The bids were opened in public at 9:00 AM on the 9th of this month. Municipal Government staff member Xiang Yu'en supervised the results. The Hexing factory offered a lower price, which was very close to the budget. They had also successfully constructed four municipal ferries. The Municipal Government then forwarded the bid to Hexing and signed the contract together. It is reported that the price was 21,500 yuan per boat, totaling 64,500 yuan for three boats. The Jiangnan factory offered 27,500 yuan per boat, a difference of 6,000 yuan, totaling 18,000 yuan for three boats.

The Municipal Public Utility Bureau Urges and Greatly Improves Beverages 178

Jinan University has a flowing well to supply the entire school with drinking water. The Municipal Public Utility Bureau had previously sent a letter to the school authorities requesting registration in accordance with the owner's self-built water supply equipment registration method. The school did not respond. In mid-June, the bureau, together with the Health Bureau, sent staff to inspect the water and take samples for testing. The results showed that the well water quality was not suitable for drinking. The Public Utility Bureau then sent a letter instructing that the well water must be oxygenated to remove iron and filtered before it can be drunk. Otherwise, a new well must be opened (Zhenru has not been included in the water supply area of any municipal water company) to obtain a good beverage. It is now learned that the school is negotiating with Zhonghua Machine Well Drilling to drill a new well. The bureau has sent another letter urging the completion of the project within one month to register and obtain a license in order to emphasize public health.

Livestock Slaughter Statistics for May and June in the City 179

The Municipal Health Bureau conducts livestock inspections, dividing them into pre-slaughter and post-slaughter inspections. For livestock transported from the Chinese area to the concession areas for slaughter, pre-slaughter inspections are carried out. For those slaughtered in the Chinese area, post-slaughter inspections are carried out. According to the bureau's inspection statistics for May and June, the number of livestock inspected in May before slaughter were: 50,256 pigs, 4,946 cattle, and 3,440 sheep. Those inspected after slaughter were: 27,864 pigs, 759 cattle, and 1,236 sheep.

Page 16

In June, pre-slaughter inspections included 456,769 pigs, 4,508 cattle, and 1,922 sheep. Post-slaughter inspections included 25,913 pigs, 1,162 cattle, and 1,253 sheep. In total, for both months, the inspections covered 1,498,025 pigs, 11,375 cattle, and 7,851 sheep.

Yongjia County Government Requests the Transfer of Yan Shibao 180

Claiming Yan Shibao is a major suspect in a certain case, but the police have determined his behavior to be proper.

The Yongjia County Government reported that Shanghai resident Yan Shibao, residing on Xinji Bang Road in Hongkou, Shanghai, is a major suspect in a certain case in the county. They specifically requested the Special District Local Court to issue a warrant for Yan's arrest so that he could be transferred. At that time, Wei Yinde, a lawyer for the police, appeared in court to object, stating that the police investigation revealed that Yan had resided in the concession for many years and his usual behavior was considered proper. The inland government has not yet presented evidence of a crime. For the sake of protecting law-abiding residents of the concession, he opposed the transfer. The judge then instructed that the matter be investigated and verified. Subsequently, the Yongjia County Government sent another document insisting on the transfer for trial. Just as Yan, having been detained for a long time, commissioned a lawyer to apply for bail, the court, due to Yongjia's insistence on the transfer, did not grant bail. Yan's lawyer then filed an appeal, stating that Yongjia County now has a formal local court, so why can the county government still handle judicial matters? Moreover, the so-called report from a secret agent lacks concrete evidence. People cannot be arrested without legal basis and should be tried in a formal court. The county government, relying solely on a blank document, designates a person as a major criminal, which is appalling. It was requested that Yongjia County be notified to order the secret agent to appear for questioning. Furthermore, Yan's neighbors and merchants jointly requested the court to allow Yan Shibao to be entrusted to the merchants for bail according to law, and they would be responsible for his appearance when summoned. This bail bond was submitted to the court yesterday, but the court's decision is unknown.

Meeting of the Shanghai Municipal Council Staff Committee 181

Gradually Abolishing the Chinese Language Allowance

The Shanghai Municipal Council Gazette stated that on Friday, August 1st, at 4:00 PM, the Council held a Staff Committee meeting. Present were Mr. Macnaghten, Mr. Carnie, Mr. Inoue, Mr. Lysaught, Mr. Liu Hongsheng, Mr. Li Ming, and Acting Head of the Accounting Department, Mr. Creer. Mr. Macnaghten, acting as chairman, approved the minutes of the previous meeting. Regarding the temporary employee Chinese language allowance case, the chairman reported that the Head of the Works Department inquired whether temporary employees of the Council should be paid a Chinese language allowance, and the Salary Committee proposed to stop issuing the allowance. A discussion was requested. Mr. Creer stated that if service personnel had not previously had this right, it was not necessary to grant it now. Given the current situation, familiarity with the Chinese language is a necessary qualification for serving in the Council, and there is no need for a separate allowance. However, when they begin their service in the various departments of the Council, the heads of each department should properly consider their starting salary and recommend them in accordance with the regulations. After discussion by the committee members, they unanimously agreed with Mr. Creer's opinion and resolved to formulate regulations to gradually abolish this system of Chinese language allowances. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Shanghai Municipal Council's Reply to the Ratepayers' Association 185

Regarding the Request to Remove Temporary Trash Cans

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Council replied to the letter from the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association stating that the letter of July 30th concerning the installation of temporary trash cans at the intersection of Sian Road and Lushun Road requested their removal. An investigation revealed that the facts disputed in Mr. Lu's letter did not match the facts verified by the Council. The accumulated garbage at that location had been treated with various disinfection methods, as mentioned in the previous letter, to prevent the breeding of flies and avoid obstruction. This method had been inspected and found to be effective. During this season, the number of flies at that location was not observed to be more than in other places. Furthermore, the trash cans were surrounded by bamboo fences, kept clean, and placed in a location that did not obstruct traffic and was near few shops. Under the current circumstances, even if citizens feel inconvenience, it is beyond the Council's power to resolve.

This intention was mentioned in the previous letter. The reply is hereby given for your information.

Production is high, demand exceeds supply, additional shares are issued to expand.

The Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Co., Ltd. has been established for a year, and its printed cotton cloth is very popular. Recently, because the demand exceeds supply, the output is insufficient for distribution. The shareholders' meeting resolved to add 35 yuan of capital to expand the business. Last night at 6:00 PM, a special reception was held at the Atlantic Restaurant for people from all walks of life, and samples of the products were displayed in the venue for reference. More than 200 representatives from various industries attended. Chairman Zhang Rongchu delivered a speech stating that the company has been established for more than a year, and recently, due to business development, shares have been issued. He hoped that people from all walks of life would strongly promote domestic products to solve people's livelihood problems. Yang Qingpan then introduced Han Yougang, the representative of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, who praised the company's development of industry and the excellent quality of its products. Each attendee was given a piece of fabric as a souvenir. The company's factory is located at No. 1382 Gaolang Bridge, Huade Road. It has built more than 70 factory buildings, purchased more than 100 printing and dyeing machines, and employs more than 400 workers. Since January of this year, monthly output has gradually increased, with an average daily output of more than 90,000 yards of printed cloth. As a result, imported printed cloth has been greatly reduced. The raw materials used are all produced by the Housheng Yarn Factory. At present, there are more than 250 kinds of satin cloth, flower label cloth, and flower yarn, with bright colors and lower prices than foreign goods. The attached picture shows the working situation of the printing and dyeing machine in the factory.

People in Songkou who heard about it came to see it, but they were afraid and did not dare to approach it. The ship sailed to Shanghai last night and docked at Pudong.

Police Investigate Tax Evasion by Watermelon Boats 196

The Old Gate Bridge section of the Suzhou Creek is a gathering place for various fruit and vegetable boats. Since watermelons came on the market, the creek has been filled with boats loaded with watermelons. Most of the boatmen who should pay taxes do not pay them to the tax authorities. They rely on the fact that both banks belong to the concession areas. After selling the watermelons, they untie the boats and leave, without ever setting foot in the Chinese area, so the tax authorities can do nothing. The Municipal Public Security Bureau believes that this long-term tax evasion is detrimental to sovereignty. Therefore, six police officers were specially dispatched to investigate yesterday. The police officers initially stood on the riverbank of North Suzhou Road. Seeing that the police officers were all in uniform, the patrolmen of the administering police station reported this to their chief, who notified the police officers that they were not allowed to perform their duties in the concession. Thereupon, the police officers all stepped onto the boats loaded with watermelons and investigated them one by one.

Lin Yuanceng, the owner of a certain inn in the French Concession, yesterday brought Liu Songlin, an employee, to the French court, accusing him that in the past month, because five tourists wanted to go to Guangdong, the merchant ordered the defendant to buy five boat tickets on their behalf. The merchant first sent the five tourists to the steamer. Afterwards, the ship set sail, and Liu returned to the inn and said that the boat tickets had been handed over to the tourists. The merchant believed him to be true. Unexpectedly, the merchant received a letter from the tourists yesterday, saying that they had not received the boat tickets and had purchased them separately. When Liu Songlin was asked, he gave vague answers, obviously embezzling. Therefore, he brought the case to court and requested an investigation. Now there is a letter as proof to be presented. When questioned, Liu Songlin admitted that the merchant really had used the money for the boat tickets for his own purposes because he was poor and had no choice. The judge Zhu sentenced the defendant to embezzlement and ordered him to be imprisoned in the Western Prison for one month to serve as a warning.

Embezzling, sentenced to imprisonment in the Western Prison

He requested a strict arrest, etc. The French police arrested Wang and seized only 350 yuan of stolen money. More than 800 yuan was missing. He was taken to the police station and sent to the French court for investigation yesterday. The plaintiff accused Wang of embezzling funds privately and requested the recovery of the stolen money. When questioned, Wang Laoer admitted that he had privately used the funds because he had lost 50 yuan at the time. He was afraid and did not dare to return to the shop, so he went to the gambling house in hopes of winning back the money, but he lost more than 200 yuan instead. In addition, he heard the news of his mother's death and immediately returned to his hometown to take care of the funeral, so a total of more than 800 yuan had been used up. He now had no ability to repay and begged for leniency. Judge Zhu sentenced him that the defendant's crime of embezzlement was established, and he was ordered to be imprisoned in the Western Prison for six months to serve as a warning. The stolen money was ordered to be returned to the plaintiff.

40 Yuan Was Hell Money and Counterfeit Money

However, the afternoon before yesterday, Ms. Jin took these banknotes out to go shopping and was seen by someone to have 40 yuan in hell money and counterfeit money. The remaining 20 yuan was definitely genuine money. Ms. Jin was very angry when she heard the news and invited Zhao Shouxin, who had witnessed the payment of the money, to testify with her and arrested Dong Baomin, calling the police together and arresting him. The police of the Sixth District accused Dong of switching the real banknotes, defrauding, and taking money. News from Various Unions 207

The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Federation of Textile Mill Workers' Unions Addresses a Letter to Fellow Workers in Foreign-Owned Textile Mills: Dear fellow workers, China is suffering from the political aggression and economic oppression of imperialists. All undertakings are suppressed by imperialists and cannot develop freely. In particular, we toiling workers are trapped by our circumstances and compelled by our livelihoods to suffer their direct and indirect torment. This is indeed the most unfortunate of misfortunes. China is known as a nation of 400 million people with vast lands and abundant resources, coveted by all countries. Why should we be dominated by these small nations? This is truly a strange and heartbreaking matter. Generally, the creation of all things must first have a cause before there can be a result. China has reached this state, and there must be a cause before this result can be realized. To investigate the cause, we should consider several major aspects. To build a strong and prosperous nation, one must observe the nature of its people, the condition of its land, and the level of its industries. Now, considering our own China, although the population is large, everyone clings to family concepts and does not extend their thoughts to the nation or the world, regarding everyone outside the family as outsiders, thus creating a sense of discrimination and no mutual assistance or unity to speak of. Therefore, even with 400 million compatriots, we cannot unite to form a powerful nation. Foreigners often use the phrase "a sheet of loose sand" to mock the people's inability to unite, fundamentally losing the heart of patriotism. If the people do not know the nation, how can the nation protect the people? This is generally the case with the Chinese people. Next, speaking of the land, China's land is fertile and produces abundant resources, especially minerals. Unfortunately, they are not exploited, but lie hidden in the earth unused. Although there are a few places where exploitation has begun, most of the major shareholders are foreigners, and great power is lost without recovery. Much of the fertile land in the interior remains uncultivated, and the people suffer from famine, leaving fertile land unused. Therefore, although China's land is vast, it is largely wasteland. How can we speak of great benefits? Industry is the key to a developed nation. Any nation seeking wealth and power must first develop its domestic industries. Since the opening of trade, China's industries have suffered greatly, and in recent years, the situation has deteriorated. The biggest reasons for this decline are nothing more than the exploitation, manipulation, and competition by imperialists. Taking Shanghai as an example, many tobacco factories, silk factories, and textile mills have suffered losses and closed down due to competition from foreign merchants, leaving hundreds of thousands of workers unemployed. Is this not a fatal blow to China's industries? If we do not take swift measures, the future dangers will be even more severe, and recovery will be even more difficult. In this autumn of declining industries, I wonder what Chinese capitalists and the government will think? After looking at the above points, we naturally feel a hundred and twenty thousand times of pain and a hundred and twenty thousand times of panic. So, how should we, the compatriots working in foreign-owned textile mills, arouse our conscience and how should we find ways to remedy the situation to avoid the future danger of becoming slaves of a conquered nation? I know that imperialists make considerable profits every year by establishing factories in China. These are purely the crystallization of our workers' blood and sweat. Otherwise, how could a few machines and a few foreigners earn so much money? Of course, they rely on our toiling workers to work hard. Logically, how should those foreign capitalists improve our treatment and how should they care for us to alleviate the suffering of our laborers? However, foreign capitalists, devoid of humanity and with hideous faces, only know how to seek their own interests, treating workers like cattle and horses, often beating and scolding them, and even dismissing them. Our toiling workers are trapped in a dilemma for the sake of their livelihoods, daring to be angry but not daring to speak out. This not only makes you indignant, but even outsiders express great excitement. At a time when oppression is increasing, our only solution is to unite all workers and concentrate our strength. The pain we have suffered in the past is all because we were too scattered. As the saying goes, a single arrow is easily broken, but a crowd is difficult to crush. There are no less than hundreds of thousands of textile mill workers in Shanghai. With such a large foundation, and with a spirit of hard work and firm unity, is it not enough to deal with a small number of imperialist capitalists? This association is now preparing to organize the Shanghai Federation of Textile Mill Workers' Unions under the order of the Municipal Party Department, as a large group of textile mill workers in the city. We hope that all workers will awaken together and work under the leadership of our party to carry out the workers' revolution, seek the liberation of workers, abolish all kinds of harsh treatments, and promote the awakening of capitalists. This is the only way out for all of us workers. Our slogan is that all textile mill workers in the city should unite to seek a way out for the workers. To seek our liberation, we must first unite and awaken ourselves. It is our responsibility to unite together to demand improved treatment, save the country, and fight for survival.

The Cantonese Cuisine Restaurant and Teahouse Dim Sum Union held an executive committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Liang Yongyi reported on the work (omitted) as usual. The Tailors' Union held an emergency joint meeting yesterday. Chairman Ruan Xinfa discussed the following matters: 1. The Shanghai Volunteer Fire Brigade had previously dismissed five workers, including Zhou Baoling, without reason and refused to grant them retirement benefits. The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association had forwarded the matter to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, ordering them to comply. However, the union recently received a letter from the brigade stating that it was difficult to comply due to regulations. A discussion was held on how to negotiate the matter. It was resolved to send a letter urging them to make a firm effort to negotiate with the Shanghai Municipal Council and to fill out a mediation application form and submit it to the Social Affairs Bureau to forward it to the Mediation Committee to seek a method to achieve twice the result with half the effort. [T13]2[/T] The term of office for the second executive committee of the union is about to expire, and a motion was made to schedule a re-election. It was resolved that the venue for the third election would still be at the Changsheng Public Hall on Huiwen Road North. The date of the general meeting will be decided and announced by the next standing committee meeting. [T13]3[/T] The Western Clothing Trade Association replied to the union's request for a salary increase with rejecting wording. A discussion was held on how to negotiate the matter. It was resolved to continue to argue based on reason. [T13]4[/T] The monthly fee income for this month is very low and insufficient for public use. A discussion was held on how to handle this. It was resolved that all executive committee members would be responsible for temporarily compensating for the deficit and reimbursing them when the autumn collection is made. All members passed the resolution, and the meeting adjourned.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin will be hot and cloudy with thunderstorms. There will be summer seasonal winds along the coast of the country. A hurricane in the Pacific Ocean is turning northwest. On the same day last year, the highest was 81.7 degrees and the lowest was 71.1 degrees.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Letters of a Young Girl 209

— Chun

Written by Xia Zhongdao

In such a patriarchal society with deeply rooted and unbreakable feudal ethics, while the huge waves of new ideas are rapidly stirring the hearts of young people who are eager to fight for their own freedom and happiness and to seek the expression of their natural love, the tragic phenomenon inevitably appearing in this transitional period seems to be unfolding both plainly and dramatically. This is indeed a major and fatal injury to the general young people of modern times who are burning with the flames of youth. After encountering the attack of these shackles, what kind of impact do many promising young people have? How great is the pain deep in the hearts of young people caused by this huge catastrophe? Unfortunately, the liberation of thought bestowed upon young people by the May Fourth Movement has continued to develop in a deformed manner. The reform of the real social system has been completely abandoned. Young people in this transitional era, on the one hand, the awakening of reason forms an emotion that they are unwilling to lag behind and struggle, burning straight from head to toe, but after the struggle, they find that there are more obstacles ahead. As a result, the initially resolute courage disappears unconsciously, and the sea of ​​frustration follows, and even doubts arise about the so-called existence, falling into confusion. The old-fashioned national character of our ancient Eastern country is that the performance of emotional warmth and activism is rarely seen, and most of them are nothing more than self-pity and blaming fate.

Regarding this kind of fact reflected in literary works, there have indeed been many in recent years, but the content is all moans after being tired of struggling. Knowing that they should struggle, they are also afraid of the harshness of the real environment and tacitly admit defeat. Therefore, in order to vent their grief and indignation, they present everything to society, hoping to gain sympathy. However, although such typical characters are affectionate, they are actually hypocritical and have a bad influence on readers.

This book, "Letters of a Young Girl," is also a cry squeezed out under the pressure of the feudal family system, but it is a struggle for the active. Such a typical character is what we currently require. She is not as unmotivated as the general trend. She clearly recognizes her own path and always grasps the hints of light, declaring war on the environment with wisdom.

This collection includes fifty-six short letters. Except for fifteen letters to her lover, the rest are to her friends. The general plot is like this:

She and Xuan Yi were engaged as children when they were still young. The tender shoots of their love also raced against time, building the foundation of a pyramid. Who would have thought that her father would unfortunately pass away, encountering the collapse of the money shop, and then the house in Chengdu would be destroyed by fire, just like being washed away by a flood. Fortunately, there was some ancestral property in the countryside that could barely support their lives. He was willing to live a life of labor and agriculture at home, so her father, who was infatuated with power, wanted to break off the engagement and find someone else. Naturally, she strongly resisted, but his attitude towards this incident was very pessimistic. She said in a letter to Ru Li: How can I blame him? Nowadays, women are indeed too materialistic. Naturally, I am not considered too materialistic either. When this incident first happened, he didn't care about it in his heart, or thought it was an inevitable trend. On the one hand, he had no power to argue, and on the other hand, he was quite suspicious of me. If I hadn't taken the initiative to resist, we would have been unknowingly isolated, which is unknowable. She discovered that it was the cannibalistic ethics, especially her relatives, who were cannibals. Her pockmarked aunt, Tu Gaoshi, wanted to marry the daughter of the Gao family for their power and influence. The Gao family used this as an exchange condition, wanting her to come out and help them consolidate the marriage. They also threatened that if she didn't agree, they would pursue the three thousand taels of dowry subsidy that her grandmother had promised her when she was alive. The rumors became tighter and tighter every day, but she resolutely said, "As long as my life force is not extinguished, I must fight with my life. Rather than live in shame, I would rather give up my life to protect my complete personality and the justice of life." She decided to run away. Unexpectedly, she hesitated to inquire about the truth of their farce and hid in a tenant's house in a relatively remote area eight or nine miles away, but the news leaked out and she was found and taken back. This was terrible. She violated her parents, and you know what crime she committed. "Father asks son to die, son dares not disobey." What is a small sin worth? It is worse than raising pigs. "Daring to ruin the family reputation, I regret giving birth to such an evil thing and throwing it into the toilet." She was beaten and confined in a secret room with no ventilation. After being confined for three days, she had no choice but to use the means of feigned surrender to carry out her second escape. When her family was unprepared, she escaped from the tiger's mouth again. On the road, she met two women who were almost in the same predicament. When she arrived in Shanghai, she was repeatedly encouraged and invited by her friends to go to Nanyang to be isolated from her motherland and drift to the ocean islands to live a new life.

The first to twentieth letters are reflections of frustration, the twenty-first to thirty-second letters are formal declarations of war against ethics, and the thirty-third to fifty-sixth letters are the hardships of the journey and the hardships of the journey. At the same time, she has a deeper understanding of the current state of society and feels that there is no second way for our young women to find a way out except to participate in the actual revolution (page 76). She realized that the status of women's movement activists in society is only regarded as entertainers by the general public. The reason is nothing more than that some people are always unwilling to improve and never read books, and they don't even have the ability to promote themselves. Young people engage in social interactions publicly, but what kind of social interactions are they, specifically focusing on love (page 84)? Therefore, we must instill revolutionary consciousness, at least to think of appropriate ways to survive for ourselves (page 104). Secondly, it is pushed to the entire women's issue. Indeed, in the environment where modern women are in this new misunderstanding and the old is still unable to be liberated, it is already difficult to get rid of it, and dare to say freedom and equality (page 93)? Therefore, we can only rely on our own efforts and use active self-defense methods to protect ourselves (page 93). The special characteristic of her personality is that she can understand everything and analyze it. Although she still cannot avoid believing that fate is my prejudice, and this prejudice occupies the part of my heart and is firmly rooted (page 66). Whether the existence of actual fate is really incomprehensible. Even if the will is strong, it is natural to admit the dominance of fate at a certain period. What is valuable is to be able to fight against fate instead of doubting and discouraging oneself.

Secondly, we can see her conditions for love. I don't believe that love must be built on money (page 2), but he shows the infinite fortitude and courage of a young man. He does not have the strange habits of a spoiled young master. His personality and status have a particularly deep impression on me (page 9). Moreover, life can only be said to be happy if it is not subject to frustration in the spirit or condemnation in the conscience. What is the enjoyment of the body? What is the possession of property (page 6)? He is willing to put down his identity to work hard, not asking anyone for a penny to support his old mother, and he also wants to send his sister to school (page 5). Therefore, this spirit of enduring hardship and hard work really makes me admire him to the extreme. I can't find a second person in the world who deserves my respect and love except him (page 8). She is even more heartbroken that women in this 20th century who advocate liberation and transformation still have the same psychology as women without knowledge in the past. Let alone those who have received considerable education, at least they must give up vanity and dependence to be able to speak. Who knows, it is not only inferior but also excessive. If there is a possibility of choice for men, then the status and money of men fill her lungs (page 31). Then what should the young people of the era think?

According to Xia Zhongdao Jun's preface, this was a letter given to him from Singapore, and it was attached with a draft. The letter is like this: "Sir, I am very sick now, and the doctors' expressions are very unusual. Isn't my misfortune caused by myself? There is more than one Shuli who has been sacrificed under the old family system. One death is not enough. It's just pitiful that I'm just like a cold sigh with exhausted energy. I venture to ask you to write a small book for me, hoping to leave some traces of my struggle to the end, indicating that I am not a weakling." (Here, Xia Jun has adapted the letter draft.)

As for here, there is no so-called skill or structure. What can move people is the burning and tearful, intense enthusiasm. It is even more sufficient to stir people's resonance because it comes from the cry of a young girl. Although the narration is mixed and there are many places with verbose words, this is not important. The more it expresses the true feelings of a young girl.

Indeed, what is the world without light, without flowers, and without love (page 17)? If the old society is not destroyed quickly, the women who are killed will only increase day by day (page 90). In fact, is it only the women's side in this era? I think it should be supplemented as: If the old society is not destroyed quickly, the young people who are killed will only increase day by day.

The Story of World Literature (188) 212

— Written by American John Macy, Translated by Hu Zhongchi

Chapter 48: The Poetry of America

Yes, heaven is yours, but this is the world of light and darkness. Our flowers are just flowers, and the shadow of your complete happiness is our light. If I could live where Asraffill lived, and he could live where I live, he would not sing the terrible tune so well, and a more exciting tune would be emitted from my harp into the great sky.

Poe's instinct and ambition were the instinct and ambition of a poet, but we often see poets writing excellent prose. When Poe descends into novels and criticisms with smaller harmonies, he exerts his genius. We have already said a lot about his prose in other chapters. Here, we will only think that even if his lyric poems are destroyed, the prose writer will still be left behind.

America's poet laureate is Longfellow. He maintained the most gentle and humble dignity and sat on that democratic throne for several years. He wrote many American legends such as "Hiawatha," "The Courtship of Miles Standish," "The Wreck of the Hesperus," and "Paul Revere's Ride," and also dedicated more (and much richer) translations and adaptations of European literature. In addition, he also created ballads and lyric poems that are like the famous "Psalm of Life," with no space or time. "Psalm of Life" is an ordinary problem that does not rise to the realm of true lyric poetry by any miracle of words or melody. His "Village Blacksmith" is a work published in the poetry column of rural newspapers, but it is excellent in technique. This is because Longfellow is an artist who understands the art of poetry processing. The masterpiece of this most popular American poet is the translation of Dante's "Divine Comedy," and the thing closest to originality he wrote with a majestic pen is the short poem he attached to the Italian poet's ode. The explanation for the above seems to be that the professor poets in New England knew the inferiority of their literature and went to Europe to seek inspiration. The bones in armor were somewhat of a failure, as was the gallows of the crane, but the belfry of Bruges was a beautiful ballad.

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest domestic and foreign publications. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, and educational books and newspapers are included in the introduction, but boring books will not be introduced.

The pictures are limited to the latest works of new domestic and foreign artists and accompanying pictures related to the text.

(2) Texts about the textual research or research of ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(3) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(4) Each text should not exceed 3,000 words.

Art Circle

Recent Developments in Norwegian Literary Circles 214

— Changxi

Nationalistic Literary Masterpieces of Norway

Norway in My Heart

In recent years, several countries in the Scandinavian Peninsula have occupied a significant position in the world literary scene. Their writers possess a distinctive style, noticeably different from writers in other nations. Due to their geographical location, it's not only difficult for their works to be recognized globally, but even within their own country, printing difficulties and a small readership often lead to their obscurity in a land shrouded in half-year darkness.

However, recently, there has been a remarkable cultural surge in that peninsula, with literature serving as the primary driving force. Last year, publications in neighboring Holland marked a new era for the literary world. The enthusiastic sales of literary books during the Norwegian Christmas season were unprecedented in the country. As William Nygarad, a leader in the publishing industry, stated, "When the long winter nights arrive, lamps are lit, and the Norwegian people eagerly seek books to while away the long nights. But in spring and summer, as daylight lengthens and nights become brighter, their interests shift to other pursuits." Therefore, he pointed out that books sell easily in autumn and winter, especially around Christmas when gift-giving is at its peak, providing a time for literary figures to gain fame and status, and for publishers to enjoy their most prosperous business.

Amidst the surge of enthusiastic sales during last year's Christmas season, many writers actively sought to solidify their position in this trend. However,

Hamsun

(Knut Humsun) could never break free from his eccentric personality, and his isolation made him inaccessible to many. Even on his 70th birthday, he fled to the seaside. Nevertheless, writers prepared a commemorative silver cup as a gift for him, making his birthday meaningful. Although he remained solitary and silent, without new works to contribute to bookstores, two books are worth mentioning: a large commemorative book printed in folio to celebrate his 70th birthday, and an expanded biography by Einarh Snlan.

At the same time, a female writer comparable to this solitary author,

Undset

(Signd Undest), deserves attention. She is one of the most diligent Norwegian writers. In addition to her three-volume historical novel set in the Middle Ages, *The Master of Hestwiken*, she recently released a novel called *Gymnadenia*, which stands in stark contrast to the three volumes about ancient times. This novel is a narrative of modern stories and is said to represent the first work in her changed style. Although the publishers in Oslo gave it a lukewarm reception, the first edition of 10,000 copies sold out in less than three days.

On the other hand, works by many established writers have been critically acclaimed in the Norwegian literary scene. The works of the well-known to Chinese readers,

Bojer

(Johan Bojer), namely *Folk ved sjoen* published in 1929, was regarded by enthusiastic writers and readers as the most beautiful creation among all his works. At the same time, *Medmennesker* by Dus (Olav Auun) and *Vore Gyerminger* by 愛季 (Peter Egge) also occupied an important place in this wave.

Among many productions, Norway, like Holland and Sweden, is experiencing a frenzy of translated works surpassing those by native authors. Therefore, many

English and American translated works

are also published in Norwegian literary circles. For example, Martha Ostenson's recent *The Young May Moon* has been translated into Norwegian by C G Hambro. Among many translations, this one has been introduced very successfully. At the same time, two works describing the stories of Norwegian Americans are worth introducing: Knut Wiswick served in the Canadian army and recently wrote about his experience in *Fra mennesk til Soldat*. Because of his vivid depiction of war and soldier life, he has been called the Norwegian Remarque. In addition, Waldemar Ager also published a novel, *Hundeoine*, about the experiences of Norwegians living in Chicago in the United States. These are all creations with a strong foreign flavor, between domestic and translated works in Norwegian literature, and are regarded as marking a new era.

In addition to these works of fiction, what is ultimately worth introducing is the work in the field of

Norwegian Poetry.

Nordabl Grieg Norway enjoys great fame in modern poetry. His short song *Norgl ivaare hjeter* is full of irrepressible nationalism and has won enthusiastic acclaim. Herman Widenvey is a leading Norwegian poet and is called Heine the Second. Therefore, he has endeavored to translate Heine's collection of short songs from 1827, *Buch der Lieder*, into Norwegian, further making him famous because of Heine.

In terms of novels and poetry, Norway has indeed made great progress. However, in addition to focusing on modern efforts, it is also paying attention to the cultural influences of the past on modern threads. In order to show the annual progress of the publishing industry, they are holding a

Norwegian Book Exhibition

in Oslo, which offers a glimpse into the development of Norwegian culture from 1829 to 1929. In the university library in the capital city, the arrangement of books from this century shows that the annual publications one hundred years ago were only one hundred, and now they have exceeded it by twelve times. This clearly shows how Norway, with less than three or four million people, has made a sudden leap in culture, and that novels, biographies and travelogues are in greater demand compared to books on thought and theory.

Literary Anecdotes

Edgar Allan Poe Society Essay Contest 215

The Edgar Allan Poe Society will award a prize of $100 annually for critical essays on Poe's works, starting this year. The essays should not exceed 2,000 words and must be submitted by the end of April of the same year. Poe had wanted to start a magazine discussing literature, art, politics, and drama, but his wish was not fulfilled. Recently, his relatives, Mrs. Wilson and Ms. Elizabeth Poe, jointly launched a bi-monthly magazine named *Stylus*. The statement in the first issue stated that Poe's literary theories for this ideal magazine during his lifetime are still correct, and there is still a place for such a publication in American literature. The magazine plans to have awards for each issue related to Poe. The first issue is a poem with Poe as the theme, with a first prize of $50 and second and third prizes of $25 each.

The Author of "Five and Ten" 216

Fannie Hurst, the author of the recently published *Five and Ten*, is already considered a well-known female writer. However, there is an interesting story. After her first novel was published, she, like many writers, personally visited bookstores to see if her book was prominently displayed and selling well. She walked into the first one and couldn't see a single copy. When she asked, the clerk told her that they didn't have the book yet, but it would be available in two or three days. She went back to ask again that week, and the clerk still replied that they didn't have the book. "It's strange, someone has already asked about this book twice this week." This shows how difficult it is for a writer to become famous.

Jiaotong University Girl Receives Award: Rosary Commemorative Pin 217

Since Vice President Li took office at Jiaotong University last year, he has advocated soliciting donations from outsiders to award prizes to the school's female students, rewarding the top-performing female students to encourage them to study hard and develop women's transportation education. Since the solicitation, Mr. Li Shengzhi of Guangdong has donated 200 silver dollars annually to commemorate his late wife, Ms. Liu Nianzhu, to make a gold pin named Nianzhu Commemorative Pin, specially awarded to one of the Jiaotong University female students with the best average grade each academic year. In the seventeenth year, Ms. Li Xuan of the first year of preparatory school was expected to be the best performing female student in the school. In the first semester of the seventeenth year, she obtained a total average of 91 points, and 90.3 points in the second semester, averaging 90.65 points, making her the female student with the best overall grade in the school. Therefore, Vice President Li awarded Ms. Li the Nianzhu Commemorative Pin at the graduation ceremony last month. Ms. Li is naturally intelligent and has a good foundation in various subjects. Because she had finished the second grade at Zhongxi High School and entered Jiaotong University only in the first year of preparatory school, she has been more than capable in all subjects and has achieved such good grades, which are highly praised by the general teachers. When she went on stage to receive the award, the whole hall applauded and laughed, because this was the first time that a female student at Jiaotong University had won an award. Ms. Li's achievements are also the first time in history that a female student has exceeded 90 points. It is rumored that Ms. Li intends to enter the Department of Electrical Engineering and will become an electrical scholar in the future, allowing Chinese women to occupy a place in the field of engineering. (Quan)

Statistics on Jiaotong University Examination Candidates 219

Jiaotong University's enrollment examinations in Shanghai, Beijing, Guangzhou, Wuhan, and Shenyang were completed on the 26th. Examination papers from all locations were specially sealed with sealing wax and mailed to the Shanghai headquarters. The admissions committee hired Mr. Hu Dunfu to grade mathematics scores, Mr. Qiu Weiyu to grade physics scores, Mr. Xu Mingcai to grade chemistry scores, Mr. Chen Jiayou to grade Chinese scores, Tang Moubo to grade English, and Li Quanshi to grade economics, business history, geography, and other scores. All scores have been graded and the names of the newly admitted students will be announced in newspapers at the examination locations at home and abroad in a day or two. The following are the statistics of this examination obtained through special investigation:

(1) There were more than 2,700 candidates, with Shanghai having the most, accounting for slightly more than 65%, and Shenyang having the fewest, accounting for slightly less than 7%. Girls accounted for 8% of the total, with Beijing girls accounting for the most, accounting for 75% of all girls, and the ratio of girls to boys in that area was 8 to 9.

(2) There were 105 admitted students, accounting for 4% of the total number of applicants. Only five of them were female, accounting for slightly less than 4% of the total number of female applicants. The ratio of admitted boys to girls was 1 to 20.

(3) There were more than 460 participating schools, with Shanghai having the most, with more than 310 schools, accounting for slightly less than 68% of the total.

(4) There were more than 250 admitted schools, accounting for slightly more than 54% of the total. Among them, there were more than 180 schools in Shanghai alone.

(5) Yangzhou High School had the best results, with 50 candidates and 18 admissions, accounting for 36%. The average score of the candidates was also the highest for Yangzhou High School students, with a score of more than 78 points. (Quan)

Letter 222

To the Editor,

According to Mr. Yu, the person in charge of the Hongye Painting and Calligraphy Society, he was surprised to read the article in the Shanghai Market column of your newspaper on August 4, which stated that the Hongye Painting and Calligraphy Society was organized by Han Guojun, Tan Hailing, Jiang Zishu, Zhao Banbo, Wang Wei, Wang Xishen, and other thirty celebrities. After investigation, the Hongye Painting and Calligraphy Society is an organization of Yu Ligeng, Xue Feibai, and Jiang Hengyuan. All celebrities who have joined the society are listed in the position of supporters, not organizers. There are discrepancies and actual interests involved. We have entrusted our lawyer to write to you and request a correction as soon as possible. Therefore, on behalf of them, we submit this letter and hope you will investigate and make the correction.

Lawyer Yu Zufeng, sincerely, 19, 8, 13.

(Statement) After investigation, the manuscript of the Hongye Painting and Calligraphy Society has the seal of Han Guojun as a mark. This publication only added the word "announced." The words "This society is organized by Han Guojun...and other thirty celebrities" are all original text. This publication has not added a word or subtracted a word. In addition to publishing the lawyer's letter, we hereby declare this.
